[5,3.64cd_5,3.67cd]	ātma aṃśe avasitāḥ hi eṣā mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi buddhi vat caitra ādi pratyayānām ca nirālambanatā yadi dharma bhūtā na gṛhyeta sādhana utthitayā dhiyā tatas viṣaya nānā tvāt pratiyogi anirākṛtā rūpāt sa ālambana prāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate yadi pratyaya śabdaḥ api pratyaya tvena gṛhyate saṃvitti ālambana tvam ca vāryate siddha sādhanam 
[5,3.68ab_5,3.70cd]	buddhi utpādana śaktiḥ ced vāryā sādhayam na sidhyati sādhanasya prayogaḥ atra bodhaka tvāt vinā na te na ca abhidhā asti asambandhāt ṛte bhedāt ca na asti asau na ca asau tad gatam bhedam bodhayantya dhiyā vinā prāśnikaiḥ agṛhīte ca vākyasya avayave pṛthak pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini 
[5,3.71ab_5,3.73cd]	sādhanasya aprayogaḥ syāt abhyupetya ucyate yadi pūrva abhyupagamena eva pratijñā bādhyate tatas dharma adharma ādi bhede ca na asiddhe paramārthataḥ śiṣya ātmanoḥ ca dharma ādeḥ upadeśaḥ avakalpate tad anuṣṭhānataḥ buddheḥ iṣṭaḥ bhedaḥ sphuṭam ca taiḥ sūtra antare abhyupeta tvāt bhavet āgama bādhanam 
[5,3.74ab_5,3.76cd]	sarva loka prasiddhyā ca pakṣa bādhaḥ atra te dhruvam kṛtsna sādhana buddhiḥ ca yadi mithyā iṣyate tatas sarva abhāvaḥ yatheṣṭam vā nyūna tā vā abhidhīyate teṣām sa ālambana tve vā taiḥ anaikāntikaḥ bhavet tad anyasya pratijñā ced tad anya pratyayaḥ mṛṣā tad mithyā tva prasaṅge ca sarvam pūrva na sidhyati 
[5,3.77ab_5,3.79cd]	stambha ādi sādhana jñāna bhedaḥ na hi tathā bhavet yāvat yāvat pratijñā iyam tad aṅgasya pratīyate tāvat tāvat pareṣām syāt mithyātvāt anya bādhanam viruddha avi abhicāri tvam bādhaḥ vā api anumānataḥ ittham sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyam pratisādhanam bāhya artha ālambanā buddhiḥ iti samyak ca dhīḥ iyam 
[5,3.80ab_5,3.82cd]	bādhaka apeta buddhi tvāt yathā svapna ādi bādha dhīḥ sā api mithyā iti ced brūyāt svapna ādīnām abādhanāt tasmāt sādharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavataḥ sādhane na hi vijñāna astitva bhinna tva kṣaṇika tva ādi dhīḥ tathā samyak ced abhyupeyeta tadā anaikāntikaḥ bhavet tat mithyā abhyupapattau ca pakṣa bādhaḥ prasajyate 
[5,3.83ab_5,3.85cd]	tathā ca baddham ukta ādi vyavasthā na prakalpate tatas ca mokṣa yatnasya vaiphalyam vaḥ prasajyate vikalpa utpadyamānā ca jñāna astitva ādi dhīḥ yadi mṛṣeṣṭā na ca dṛṣṭā atra pramāṇa antarataḥ gatiḥ pramāṇa abhāvataḥ tena jñāna astitva ādi durlabham sarvam ca api asmad ādīnām mithyā jñānam vikalpanāt 
[5,3.86ab_5,3.88cd]	sānnidhya viprakṛṣṭa tve sattva asattve ca durlabhe mithyājñāna aviśeṣe api sāṃkhya ādi parivarjanāt bauddha darśanaḥ ekasmin pakṣapātaḥ na yujyate mṛṣātvam yadi buddheḥ syāt bādhaḥ kim na upalabhyate bādhāt vinā api tat ced syāt vyavasthā na prakalpate pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrat jñāne mṛṣā bhavet 
[5,3.89ab_5,3.91cd]	svapna ādi buddhiḥ asmākam tava bhedaḥ api kiṅkṛtaḥ na ca anyat pratiyogi asti jāgrat jñānasya śobhanam yad darśanena mithyātvam stambha ādi pratyayaḥ vrajet svapna ādi pratiyogi tvam sarva loka prasiddhitaḥ tadīya dharma vaidharmyāt bādhaka pratyayaḥ yathā yoginām jāyate buddhiḥ bādhikā pratiyoginī 
[5,3.92ab_5,3.95ab]	jāgrat stambha ādi buddhīnām tatas svapna ādi tulya tā prāptānām tām avasthām ca sarva prāṇabhṛtām api bādhaḥ ayam bhavitā tena siddhā sa pratiyogi tā iha janmani keṣān cit na tāvat upalabhyate yogi avasthā gatānām tu na vidmaḥ kim bhaviṣyati yoginām ca asmādīyānām tvad ukta pratiyoginī tvad ukti viparītā vā bādha buddhiḥ bhaviṣyati 
[5,3.95cd_5,3.98cd]	īdṛś tve yogi buddhīnām dṛṣṭāntaḥ na tava asti ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ tu asmādīnām yaḥ gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate atha stambha ādi buddhīnām vadet sa pratiyogi tām bādhya tvam ca api buddhi tvāt mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi buddhi vat iṣṭam sa pratiyogi tvam mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi buddhibhiḥ tad ātmanā ca bādhya tvam grāhya antaratayā api ca bādhakaiḥ ca api anekāntaḥ tad anya tve ca pūrvavat 
[5,3.99ab_5,3.102ab]	mithyā adhī pratiyogi tvam svapna ādau iva te bhavet rāga ādi kṣaya yogi tva nimitta adhigatiḥ tathā yāvān viśeṣaḥ iṣṭaḥ ced sarva abhāvāt viruddha tā mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmba adhabuddhi vat vācyaḥ anumāna bādhaḥ vā yadi vā pratisādhanam pūrva sādhana doṣāḥ ca sandheyāḥ tasya ca adhunā sādhya abhedāt avācya tvāt hetoḥ na ubhaya siddha tā 
[5,3.102cd_5,3.105ab]	pratyaya tvam ca sāmānyam bhinna abhinnam na vidyate bhavataḥ atyanta bhinnam ca mad pakṣe api kathan cana sārūpya anya nivṛttī ca na iti etat sādhayiṣyate tasmāt dhetuḥ na sāmānyam asti siddham dvayoḥ api viśeṣayoḥ ca hetu tvam pakṣa tad tulya saṃsthayoḥ na syāt anvaya hīna tvāt atad dharma tayā api ca 
[5,3.105cd_5,3.108cd]	na ca artha hīnā tad buddhiḥ hetu tvena bhaviṣyati āśraya asiddhi tā ca uktā viśeṣyasya aprasiddhitaḥ tathā hetoḥ viruddha tvam dṛṣṭānte sādhya hīna tā viśeṣaṇa aprasiddha tva vikalpena eva bodhite svapna ādi pratyaye bāhyam sarvathā na hi na iṣyate sarvatra ālambanam bāhyam deśa kālāni atha ātmakam janmani ekatra bhinne vā tathā kāla antare api vā 
[5,3.109ab_5,3.112ab]	tad deśaḥ vā anya deśaḥ vā svapna jñānasya gocaraḥ alāta cakre alātam syāt śīghra bhramaṇa saṃskṛtam gandharvanagare abhrāṇi pūrva dṛṣṭam gṛha ādi ca pūrva anubhūta toyam ca raśmi tapta ūṣaram tathā mṛga toyasya vijñāne kāraṇa tvena kalpyate dravya antare viṣāṇam ca śaśasya ātmā ca kāraṇam śaśaśṛṅga dhiyaḥ mauṇḍyam niṣedhe śirasaḥ asya ca

[5,3.118cd_5,3.121cd]	bhāva antaram abhāvaḥ anyaḥ na kaḥ cit anirūpaṇāt bhavatā dvayam ati etat durnirūpam sa hetukam pratijñā doṣa vat ca api yojyā hetoḥ viruddha tā samasta vyasta dharma ādi svarūpa ādi viparyayāt dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ na hi eka vastuni tava sādhya aṃśa hetu aṃśa vyāpta dharma ādi sambhavaḥ ke cit vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ na asti iti api anuyuñjate

[5,4.165cd_5,4.168cd]	yathā eva anāgatāt jñānāt santati antara jāt api dṛḍha tvena api avijñātāt tathā utpannāt vinaśyataḥ kevala grāhaka tve tu viṣaya tvam na yujyate kim apekṣya ca tasya idam grāhaka tvam prakalpyate dvi ākāra tā nirastā eva saṃvedyeta tadā eva ca tatas ca uttara vijñānam na pratīkṣeta bodhakam dvi ākāra kalpanāyām ca parasya ātmā aṃśaḥ eva te 
[5,4.169ab_5,4.172ab]	pramāparyavasā anena na atītaḥ viṣayaḥ bhavet pūrva grāhya sarūpa tve grāhaka tvam prahīyate grāhaka ākāra mātre syāt viṣayaḥ nāsarūpataḥ na ca śakti arpaṇasya atra vyāpāraḥ upalabhyate śakti arpaṇasya ca abhāvaḥ yuṣmad pakṣe prasādhitaḥ santāna antara vat ca eṣām niṣedhyā hetu sādhya tā vāsya vāsaka bhāvaḥ ca jñāna tvāt eka santatau 
[5,4.172cd_5,4.175ab]	tasmāt yat bhāsakam rūpam tat grāhyāt tasya bhinna tā tad saṃvittau asaṃvitte rasa ādi grāhakam yathā grāhyam tat grāhakāt ca eva tad parāmṛśatā yatas na parāmṛśyate avaśyam rasa ādi grāhakam yathā dvayam paraspareṇa evam bhinnam sādhyam rasa ādi vat aika rūpyeṇa ca ajñānāt santāna antara buddhi vat 
[5,4.175cd_5,4.178cd]	jñānam sva aṃśam na gṛhṇāti jñāna utpatteḥ sva śakti vat grāhya tva pratiṣedhaḥ ca dvaya hīnāḥ hi vāsate caitra jñānam tad udbhūta jñāna aṃśa grāhya bodhakam jñāna tvāt na bhavet yadvat tasya deha antara udbhavam etayā eva diśā vācyā śakti dvaya nirākriyā pramāṇa antara siddha tvāt anyatra aneka śakti tā na tu atra kāraṇam tādṛś śakti bheda kṛt asti te 
[5,4.179ab_5,4.181cd]	tasmāt ubhaya siddha tvāt lāghavāt yaḥ parigrahaḥ upāya tvāt ca yat tasya pūrva grahaṇa kalpanam cakṣuḥ adīndriyaiḥ atra tad anaikāntikam bhavet yat api apratibaddha tvāt utpattau gṛhyatām iti tatra ātmanā na śaktyam tat na anya utpattiḥ tat asti vā tena etat kāraṇa abhāvāt tadānīm na anubhūyate 
[5,4.182ab_5,4.184cd]	na anyathā hi artha sadbhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ san upapadyate jñānam ced na iti atas paścāt pramāṇam upajāyate na ca api apratibandhena kevalena grahaḥ bhavet viśiṣṭa kāraṇa abhāve api arthaḥ na eva anubhūyate vyāpṛtam ca artha saṃvittau jñānam na ātmānam ṛcchati tena prakāśaka tve api bodhāya anyat pratīkṣyate 
[5,4.185ab_5,4.187cd]	īdṛśam vā prakāśa tvam tasya artha anubhava ātmakam na ca ātmā anubhavaḥ asti asya iti ātmanaḥ na prakāśakam sati prakāśaka tve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā rūpa ādau cakṣuḥ ādīnām tathā atra api bhaviṣyati prakāśaka tvam bāhye arthe śakti abhāvāt tu na ātmani anyena vā anubhāve asau anavasthā prasajyate 
[5,4.188ab_5,4.190cd]	tatra tatra smṛtim dṛṣṭvā sarva anubhava kalpanā ekena tu anubhūta tve sarvam tatra eva sambhavet tatra api smṛtiḥ iti etat na loka anumatam vacaḥ na hi vijñāna santānam kaḥ cit smarati laukikaḥ ghaṭa ādau agṛhīte arthe yadi tāvat anantaram arthāpattyau abudhyante vijñānāni punar punar 
[5,4.191ab_5,4.193cd]	yāvat śramam tatas paścāt tāvatī eva smariṣyati tadā tu akalpite api evam smṛti varndhyā suta ādi vat smṛti bhrāntaḥ ca yā api atra paścāt jñāneṣu jāyate tadā eva artha smṛteḥ eṣām tajñāna ādi pramāṇa tā yāvat śramam ca tad buddhiḥ tad prabandhe mahati api śramāt rucya anya samparkāt vicchedaḥ viṣayeṣu iva

[5,4.215cd_5,4.218cd]	vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyaḥ vyavasthā ākāra darśane sva pratyaya anukāraḥ hi bahu ākāreṣu vastuṣu nirdhāraṇe bhavet dhetuḥ na apūrva ākāra kalpane tathā dīrgha ghaṭa tva ādau bhinna apekṣā nibandhanā ākāra bheda sampattiḥ aviruddhā bhaviṣyati na aneka ākāra saṃvitteḥ nirākāra tva kalpanā yuktā pratīti bhedāt tu bahu ākāra tva sambhavaḥ

[5,5.20cd_5,5.23cd]	kṛta sāvayava tva ādi prayuktā ca vināśitā prayatna anantara jñāna sadṛśaiḥ na prayujyate jātimat tva indriya tva ādi vastu sanmātra bandhanam śada anitya tva siddhi artham kaḥ vadet yaḥ na tārkikaḥ tasmāt yaḥ eva yasya arthaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sādhana śaktitaḥ saḥ eva gamakaḥ tasya na prasaṅga anvitaḥ api yaḥ upāttaḥ ca eka deśābhyām dharmī api atra eka deśa tā

[5,5.27cd_5,5.30ab]	na hi tad nirapekṣa tve sambhavati anumeya tā na dharma mātram siddha tvāt tathā dharmī tathā ubhayam vyastam vā api samastam vā svātantryeṇa anumīyate eka deśasya liṅga tvam sādhyena anugamaḥ asya ca dvayam ca na syāt iṣṭam sat pakṣeṣu eṣu yathākramam anitya tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ na hi 
[5,5.30cd_5,5.33ab]	dhvaninā anugamaḥ na eṣām na ubhayasya ubhayena vā sambandhaḥ api anupādānāt nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyā api vā mitau na ca api anugamaḥ tena liṅgasya iha nidarśyate na ca ākāra dvayam tasya sādhya sādhana bhāj bhavet tasmat artha gṛhīta tvāt matubarthasya gamyatā na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā yathā daṇḍya ādi śabdataḥ 
[5,5.33cd_5,5.36ab]	viśīṣṭa artha pratītau syāt sambandhaḥ na antarīyakaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvam āpannau dvau imau atas gamyau aṅga aṅgi bhāvaḥ tu kaiḥ cit iṣṭaḥ vikalpataḥ sarvathā dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ dharmeṇa tu avagamyate viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tve na viśeṣaḥ avadhāryate tatra utaram vadanti anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam 
[5,5.36cd_5,5.39ab]	hetu dharmeṇa samandhaḥ tasya aprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ pradhāna tvāt dhi dharmeṇa sambandhaḥ vākyataḥ bhavet tatra asambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyaḥ asau dharminā saha dhvaneḥ iti atha vā vācyam anvayasya tu darśane bheda upāttasya dharmasya guṇa abhāvaḥ na duṣyati agneḥ deśa viśiṣṭa tve na ca etat pakṣa lakṣaṇam 
[5,5.39cd_5,5.42ab]	viśiṣṭa tā asya deśena bhavet evamprakārikā yaḥ agniḥ saḥ asti kva cit deśe yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yatra tatra vā agniḥ pūrva anubhūtaḥ vā deśa mātreṇa saṅgataḥ yaḥ agniḥ saḥ anena yuktaḥ vā yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anena saḥ atha vā yaḥ ayam sa deśa mātreṇa yuktaḥ pūrveṇa vā api ayam etad deśa viśiṣṭaḥ vā yaḥ ayam agniḥ iti iha tu 
[5,5.42cd_5,5.45ab]	pūrvayoḥ siddha sādhya tvam pareṣu syāt viruddha tā vyāptiḥ etena deśena sarva agnīnām na yujyate na api pūrvasya na api eṣa vahniḥ sarvaiḥ viśiṣyate deśaiḥ pūrveṇa vā api asya na deśena viśeṣyatā etad deśa viśiṣṭaḥ ayam iti etat kathyate katham yadā deśa anapekṣaḥ agniḥ na ayam iti avadhāryate 
[5,5.45cd_5,5.48cd]	agneḥ pūrvataram ca atra deśaḥ eva avadhāryate tad jñāna kāla buddhaḥ ca na deśaḥ syāt viśeṣaṇam deśasya parvata ādeḥ tu svarūpe pāvakāt ṛte gṛhīte agni viśiṣṭasya punar jñānam na duṣyati tasmāt dharma viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameya tā sā deśasya agni yuktasya dhūmasya anyaiḥ ca kalpitā nanu śabda vat eva syāt liṅgamyam viśiṣaṇam 
[5,5.49ab_5,5.52ab]	na evam na hi atra liṅgasya śakti aneka tva kalpanā na ca tasya anumeya tvam viśeṣyaḥ ca avadhāritaḥ viśiṣṭa tvena ca ajñānāt tanmātrasya anumeya tā nanu dhūma viśeṣya tve hetoḥ pakṣa eka deśa tā na etat asti viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānya hetu tā dhūma tad jāna sambandha smṛti prāmāṇya kalpane phalena viṣaya eka tvam tad vyāpārāt purā uditam 
[5,5.52cd_5,5.55cd]	prameya dhī pramāṇa tvam bhāṣya kāraḥ tu manyate pratyakṣā niyama uktaḥ ca sarvatra eva anuṣajyate anumāna gṛhītasya tena eva pratipādanam parebhyaḥ vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ yathā uditaḥ tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhya dharmaḥ vidhīyate niyamaḥ tad vipakṣāt ca kalpyate na avirodhinaḥ asat nikṛṣṭa vācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam 
[5,5.56ab_5,5.58cd]	tādrūpyeṇa paricchittiḥ tad viparyayataḥ api ca pramitasya pramāṇe hi na apekṣā jāyate punar tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇam niṣphalam param vaiparītya paricchinne na avakāśaḥ parasya tu mūle tasya hi anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayaḥ hṛtaḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ ca ṣaṭkasya yena eva arthaḥ avadhāritaḥ 
[5,5.59ab_5,5.62ab]	tena eva uttara bādhaḥ syāt vikalpa ādeḥ asambhavāt agrāhyatā tu śabda ādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate teṣām aśrāvaṇa tva ādi viruddham anumānataḥ na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇa avagamyate sa anvaya vyatirekābhyām gamyate badhira ādiṣu tridhā śabda virodhaḥ syāt pratijña ādi vibhāgataḥ pratijñā pūrva sañjalpa sarva loka prasiddhitaḥ 
[5,5.62cd_5,5.65ab]	yāvajjīvam aham mauni iti ukti mātreṇa bādhyate sarva vākyam ṛṣā tve tu dharma uktyā eva ātma bādhanam dharmī uktyā aham yatas jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama bauddhasya śabda nitya tvam pūrva upetena bādhyate candra śabda abhidheya tvam śaśinaḥ yaḥ niṣedhati sa sarva loka siddhena candra jñānena bādhyate 
[5,5.65cd_5,5.68cd]	jñāta goga vaya ākāram prati yaḥ sādhayet idam na goḥ gavaya sādṛśyam tasya bādha upama ānataḥ geha avagata nāstitvaḥ jīvan caitraḥ yadā bahis na asti iti sādhyate bādhaḥ tatra artha āpattitaḥ bhavet agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde ca anabhidhāyake śrotra ādinā astitāyām ca śabda anitya tva sādhane śruta arthāpatti bādhaḥ atra yat ā āpta ukti nivārite 
[5,5.69ab_5,5.72ab]	divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātri bhojanam śaśaśṛṅga ādi sadbhāva virodhaḥ anupalabdhitaḥ evam ca dharma sambandha bādhaḥ tāvat udāhṛtaḥ dharma dharmī u bhayeṣām ca svarūpa sva viśeṣayoḥ śruti artha ākṣiptayoḥ vākye vācyaḥ sarva pramāṇakaḥ tṛṇa ādi vikriyā hetoḥ agni mat hima sādhane pratyakṣa avagatāt śaityāt tad viśeṣa uttha bādhanam 
[5,5.72cd_5,5.75ab]	adharmaḥ vihitaḥ duḥkham karoti alpam iti iha tu vihita tvāt adharmasya svarūpasya eva bādhanam tathā duḥkha nimitta tvam viśeṣaḥ tasya bādhyate ayathārthāḥ dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ iti ukte dvaya bādhanam svarūpa sva viśeṣābhyām tat hīmithyātva sādhanāt kṣaṇikā atyanta mithyā tve viśeṣau ca dvayoḥ iha 
[5,5.75cd_5,5.78cd]	darśanāt eka deśasya iti anena etat vyudasyate yatra ekasya ubhayoḥ vā api saṃśaya adhī vi paryayāḥ śaityāt na dāhakaḥ bahniḥ cākṣuṣa tvāt anitya tā śabdasya iti evamādau tu dvayoḥ siddhaḥ viparyayaḥ kṛtaka tva guṇa tva ādau para ukte yājñikam prati sva ukte ca evamprakāre syāt asiddhaḥ anyatarasya tu bāṣpa ādi bhāva sandigdhaḥ dvayoḥ anyatarasya vā 
[5,5.79ab_5,5.81cd]	dhūmaḥ tridhā api asiddhaḥ syāt evam tāvat svarūpataḥ ete eva prakārāḥ syuḥ āśraya asiddhi kalpane jñāte api hi svarūpeṇa na atad dharme asti hetu tā sarvatra dṛṣṭa kārya tvāt ātmā sarva gataḥ tu iti bauddham pratyāśraya asiddhaḥ laukika ādeḥ tu saṃśayaḥ bāṅmātra asiddhi mātreṇa vyavahāra aprakalpanāt 
[5,5.82ab_5,5.85ab]	dvābhyām yaḥ asattvataḥ jñātaḥ tad vacaḥ dūṣaṇam matam itarat sādhanam tu syāt vādinā yadi sādhyate nirākaraṇa siddhau vā dūṣaṇam prativādinaḥ sandeha viparīta tva hetū ca atra nirākṛtau jñāta sambandha vacanāt trayaḥ saṃśaya hetavaḥ san sādhye tad abhāve vā dvābhyām vyāvṛttaḥ eva ca dvau viruddha artha sambaddhau yau ekatra eka deśini 
[5,5.85cd_5,5.88cd]	prameya anitya tā mūrti dharmāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ dvayoḥ nitya āyatna uttha yatna uttha anityeṣu dvis anityataḥ nityāḥ bhūḥ gandhavat tvena syāt asādhāraṇaḥ tu ayam niścaya eka aṅga vaikalyāt eṣa saṃśaya kāraṇam sādhāraṇaḥ yathā dṛṣṭaḥ buddhi dvaya nimittakaḥ viruddha ekān avāpteḥ ca saṃśaye kāraṇam matam atra asādhāraṇaḥ na asti tad abhāva mukhena tu 
[5,5.89ab_5,5.92ab]	dvaya asattva virodhāt ca mataḥ saṃśaya kāraṇam sandigdha hetu tā ca eṣām viṣaya apekṣayā ucyate nirṇayasya api hetu tvam dṛṣṭam sādhya antare yatas vyavaccheda anvayau labdhvā niṣkriya ādau amūrti vat kṣiti eka deśa siddha tve gandhavat tvasya hetu tā yatra apratyakṣatā vāyoḥ arūpa tvena sādhyate sparśāt pratyakṣatā vā asau viruddha avyabhicāritā 
[5,5.92cd_5,5.95ab]	ke cit jāti antaram ca enām varṇayanti apare punar sādhāraṇa tvam aṃśena samastam vā api ananvayam pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrva uktaiḥ yasya sādhanaiḥ tat parājayataḥ kāryaḥ nirṇayaḥ bādha varjanāt kva cit saṃśaya hetū yau pratyeka tvena lakṣitau saṅghāte nirṇayaḥ tābhyām ūrdhva tā kāka vat tva vat 
[5,5.95cd_5,5.98ab]	pratyekam saṃhatau vā api gamakau avirodhinau tasmāt bhinnau viruddha arthau hetū ca atra nidarśitau ṣoḍhā viruddha tām āhuḥ caturddhā vaikadhā api vā śruti artha uktasya bādhāyām pratijñā arthasya hetunā nitya tve kṛtaka tvasya dharma bādhāt viruddha tā bādhaḥ dharma viśeṣasya yadā tu evam prayujyate 
[5,5.98cd_5,5.101cd]	arthavat śabda rūpam syāt prāc sambandha avadhāraṇāt vibhaktimat tvāt paścāt vat svarūpeṇa iti ca āśrite asvarūpa artha yogaḥ tu paścāt śabdasya dṛśyate tena prāk api sambandhāt asvarūpa artha tā bhavet iha pratyaya hetu tvāt dravya ādeḥ vyatiricyate samavāyaḥ yathā iha ayam ghaṭaḥ ityādi saṅgatiḥ atra api asamavāya tvam saṃyogasya iva sidhyati 
[5,5.102ab_5,5.104cd]	tena dharmi svarūpasya vaiparītyāt viruddha tā yat ca sat tāvat eka tvam samavāyasya kalpitam tatra saṃyoga vat bhedāt syāt viśeṣa viruddha tā nityam ātma astitā kaiḥ cit yadā sautra antikam prati sādhyate avayava abhāvāt vyoma vat dvaya bādhanam tadā ubhaya viśeṣasya bādhaḥ ayam sādhyate yadā 
[5,5.105ab_5,5.108ab]	pārārthyam cakṣuḥ ādīnām saṅghātāt śayana ādi vat śayane saṅgha pārārthyam bhautika vyāpta hetuke ātmānam prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam asaṃhata para artha tve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatā api ca anahaṅkārika tvam ca cakṣuḥ ādeḥ prasajyate gamakasya eka deśasya vyāptiḥ gamya iti bhāṣitum sādhya sādharmya vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate 
[5,5.108cd_5,5.111ab]	tatra hetu artham uddiśya sādhya upādānam iṣyate uddeśyaḥ vyāpyate dharmaḥ vyāpakaḥ ca itaraḥ mataḥ yat vṛttayoḥ prāthamyam iti ādi uddeśa lakṣaṇam tad vṛttam eva kāraḥ ca syāt upādeya lakṣaṇam vadati artham sva śaktyā ca śabdaḥ vaktra napekṣayā sādhya hetu tvam arthānām vyāpti śakti anurodhataḥ 
[5,5.111cd_5,5.114cd]	tatra ajñānāt yadā vakta sahacāra vivakṣayā viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāpta tvam vivakṣati vivakṣan api vā śabdam tat yogyam na vadet yadi ghaṭe kṛtaka nāśi tve na aśi vyāptam kṛtena vā na tadā iṣṭasya hetu tvam syāt aniṣṭasya ca eva tat tasmāt vyāpya tva rūpeṇa vācyaḥ hetu tva sammataḥ yadā samyak prayukte api vākye arthaḥ na tathā bhavet 
[5,5.115ab_5,5.117cd]	sādhya hetu ubhaya vyāpti śūnya tvāt paramārthataḥ nityaḥ dhvaniḥ amūrtta tvāt karma vat paramāṇu vat ghaṭa vat vyoma vat ca api tat asat vādinam prati dharmya siddhau api hi evam dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa tā bhavet tat sadbhāve api ca vyomni dvaya yukte api kīrtite karma ādi ālocanāt vyāptiḥ hetoḥ na asti iti varjanam 
[5,5.118ab_5,5.120cd]	vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyam apekṣyate sahabhāvi tva dṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptim na lakṣayet paraḥ sādharmya dṛṣṭāntāt tat ca na apekṣate yadā vaktā vā sahabhāvi tvam śuddham tena vadet yadā viparīta anvayam vā api tat samādhitsayā tadā pūrva jñāna upamardena vaidharmyeṇa iṣṭa sādhanam 
[5,5.121ab_5,5.124ab]	sāhitya mātram pūrva uktam hetoḥ tatra upayujyate vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ hi bhāvayoḥ yādṛś iṣyate tayoḥ abhāvayoḥ tasmāt viparītaḥ pratīyate dhūma bhāve agni bhāvena vyāpte anagniḥ tatas cyutaḥ adhūmaḥ eva vidyeta iti evam vyāpya tvam aśnute tathā anagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmaḥ tata cyutaḥ anyatra anavakāśa tvāt vyāpyate dhruvam agninā 
[5,5.124cd_5,5.127ab]	vyāpakau tu yadā ucyete bhāva abhāvau tadā tatas na eva vyāpyāt vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet tasmāt dhūmena sādhya tvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā tadā anagniḥ adhūmena vyāptaḥ vācyaḥ na ca anyathā anagnya dhūma sāhitye vyāpteḥ vā api viparyaye na prastuta upakāraḥ syāt anyat vā api prasādhyate 
[5,5.127cd_5,5.130ab]	yatra api arthasya śūnya tvam dvābhyām ekena vā bhavet yat anityam tu tat mūrtam aṇu vat buddhi vat kha vat sādhyena vyāpti siddhyā eva vyatirekaḥ atra kathyate yasya ayam na asti asau hetuḥ tena sādhyena na āpyate tena dṛṣṭe api sāhitye na sarvaḥ gamyaḥ iṣyate saha dṛṣṭiḥ na sambandhaḥ vyāptiḥ na eva ca tāvatā 
[5,5.130cd_5,5.133ab]	mūrta anitya tva yukte api tasmāt aṅgīkṛte ghaṭe karma ādau vyāpti abhāvena na dṛṣṭānta tvam iṣyate aśeṣa apekṣita tvāt ca saukaryāt ca api adarśanāt sādhane yadi api iṣṭaḥ atra vyatirekaḥ anumām prati tāvatā na hi anaṅga tvam yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate bodha prasaṅgaḥ bhedānām na ca avyāpteḥ bhaviṣyati 
[5,5.133cd_5,5.136ab]	asti sāmānyavastu eṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ke cit sādharmya dṛṣṭānte vyāptyā api kathite punar vaidharmya uktim api icchanti vyāvṛtti niyama icchayā hetau sādharmya dṛṣṭāntāt sādhyena eva avadhārite vyāvṛttiḥ sarvatas prāptā sādhya abhāve niyamyate tat tu manda phalam yasmāt pakṣe api evam nirūpitam 
[5,5.136cd_5,5.139ab]	vyāpaka abhāva mātram hi vyāpyāt nityam nivartate tasmāt yathā eva śukla tve paṭasya ukte virodhinām nivṛttiḥ na tu dairdhyādeḥ tathā atra api bhaviṣyati dvaividhyam na upapannam tu yathā eva hi agni dhūmayoḥ pratyakṣa dṛṣṭaḥ sambandhaḥ gati prāptyoḥ tathā eva hi āditye anupalabdhiḥ ced na deśe api adhunātane 
[5,5.139cd_5,5.142cd]	kva cit tatra upalabdhiḥ ced devadatte api dṛśyatām yadi dharmi antara apekṣā tatra sāmānya dṛṣṭa tā syāt agni dhūmayoḥ sā eva tasmāt evam pracakṣate pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa sambandham yayoḥ eva viśeṣayoḥ gomaya indhana tad janya viśeṣa ādi matiḥ kṛtā tad deśa sthena tena eva gatvā kāla antare api tam yadā agniḥ budhyate tasya pūrva bodhāt punar punar 
[5,5.143ab_5,5.146ab]	sandihyamāna sadbhāva vastu bodhāt pramāṇa tā viśeṣa dṛṣṭam etat ca likhitam vindhya vāsinā ākṛtyoḥ eva ca eṣā iṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit hetu sādhya vyavasthā iti viśeṣaḥ na upadarśitaḥ agni dhūma antara tve ca vācye sāmānyatas mitau sāmānya dṛṣṭam ekāntāt atra iti ādityaḥ ucyate pratyakṣa viṣaya tvam ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam 
[5,5.146cd_5,5.149cd]	vastu tvam ca atra hetuḥ vā dvayasya api abhidhīyate dhūmāt agni anumānasya vastu ālambanatā bhavet abhāva anya pramāṇa tvāt sva arthe śrotra ādi buddhi vat sāmānyasya ca vastu tvam pratyakṣa grāhya tā api ca abhāvāni aprameya tvāt asādhāraṇa vastu vat sāmānyam na anumānena vinā yasya pratīyate na ca liṅga vinirmuktam anumānam pravartate 
[5,5.150ab_5,5.153ab]	asāmānyasya liṅga tvam na ca kena cit iṣyate na ca anavagatam liṅgam kiñ cit asti prakāśakam tasya vā api anumānena syāt anyena gatiḥ punar tad utpattiḥ ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānya jñāna saṃhitāt tasya ca api anumāna tvāt bhavet liṅgena ca udbhavaḥ anumāna antarāt eva jñānena evam ca kalpane liṅga liṅgī anumānānām ānantyāt eka liṅgini 
[5,5.153cd_5,5.156cd]	gatiḥ yuga sahasreṣu bahuṣu api na vidyate atha sāmānya bhūte api liṅge anyasmāt gatiḥ bhavet pramāṇāt apramāṇāt vā tathā liṅgi gatiḥ bhavet evam api anumānasya nitya ucchedaḥ prasajyate pramāṇa antaram eva syāt sāmānyasya avabodhakam apramāṇau abuddhāt vā liṅgāt liṅgini yā matiḥ sā api mithyā bhavet nityam bāṣpa jāta agni buddhi vat 
[5,5.157ab_5,5.159cd]	nanu apramāṇa bhūtā api sambandha smṛtiḥ iṣyate yathā liṅgi gatau hetuḥ tathā liṅga gatiḥ bhavet tatra yat pūrva vijñānam tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate tad upasthāna mātreṇa smṛteḥ syāt caritārtha tā na tu liṅga gatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate tad abhāva asmṛtiḥ ca atra na kathan cit pravartate 
[5,5.160ab_5,5.162cd]	smārtam etat abhedena vijñānam iti yaḥ vadet tasya vandhyā sute api asti nūnam smaraṇa śakta tā na ca asādhāraṇaḥ artha ātmā sāmānya jñāna kāraṇam yasmāt na asya avinābhāvaḥ tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathan cana syāt vā sambandha dṛṣṭyā asau sāmānyam kṛtaka tva vat na hi asādhāraṇam vastu pūrvatra iha ca vidyate 
[5,5.163ab_5,5.166ab]	na ca api avyapadeśasya vikalpa rahitasya ca vinā pūrva anusandhānāt liṅga tvam upapadyate kalpyante ca viśeṣāḥ ye te api aliṅgam ananvayāt etasmāt eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasya api aliṅga tā sāmānya rūpa tāyām vā tathā eva anavadhāraṇam kva cit vā dṛṣṭa sambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyakaḥ bhavet sambandha anubhavaḥ avaśyam eṣitavyaḥ ca liṅganaḥ 
[5,5.166cd_5,5.169ab]	anumāna pravṛtteḥ tu prāk jñānam tatra na asti te na ca api vāsanā mātrāt liṅga jñānasya sambhavaḥ liṅgi jñānam ca tadvat syāt tri rūpāt liṅgataḥ na tat tatra abhāvasya liṅga tvam na ca asau ānumānikaḥ pramāṇa antara gamya tvāt tatra doṣaḥ na jāyate pratyakṣa avagatāt liṅgāt yasya liṅgi gatiḥ bhavet 
[5,5.169cd_5,5.172ab]	tasya na atas adhikam kiñ cit prārthanīyam prasajyate yatra api anumitāt liṅgāt liṅgini grahaṇam bhavet tatra api maulikam liṅgam pratyakṣāt eva gamyate liṅga tvam kṛtaka tva ādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā pratyakṣa tvam ca tasya iṣṭam iti dūram na gamyate evam śabda upamāna ādau sāmānya āśrayatā yatas 
[5,5.172cd_5,5.175ab]	tad daussthityena daussthityam sarvatra atas prasajyate tasmāt pratyakṣa pūrva tvam pramāṇa antaraḥ iṣyate pratyakṣa tvam ca sāmānye na anyathā hi gatiḥ bhavet pratyakṣa ālambana tvam ca viśeṣasya katham bhavet yadā vastu antara apekṣaḥ sāmānya aṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate rūpa ādayaḥ hi sāmānyam sarve nīla ādi apekṣayā 
[5,5.175cd_5,5.178cd]	sva viśeṣa anapekṣya atha nīla ādīnām samāna tā te ca api tāvat sāmānyam yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ dvi aṇukasya api yat rūpam tat dhi sādhāraṇam dvayoḥ na ca antyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ asti kasya cit na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā bhedena āgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedaḥ grāhyatām vrajet na ca bhinneṣu abhinnatva buddheḥ grāhya tva sambhavaḥ 
[5,5.179ab_5,5.182ab]	samudāyaḥ na vā api asti bhavatām na ca sarvadā sarveṣām asata arthena pratyaya utpatti sambhavaḥ na ca eka jāti yogena vinā asti samudāyatā samudāye api ca aṇu tvam na eteṣām apagacchati sāmānyam iti adṛśye api tena sāmānyaḥ eva naḥ vyāsaṅginī bhavati eṣā dhīḥ vinā api eka kalpanāt vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathā indriyaiḥ 
[5,5.182cd_5,5.185cd]	grahaṇam tadvat eva syāt prativyakti niveśinaḥ mīmāṃsakaiḥ ca na avaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ yat balena upalabdhasya mithyātvam kalpayet bhavān samūha rūpam pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ yaḥ apahnute śaśasya api saḥ abhāvam śṛṅgataḥ vadet samūha parama artha tve sthite tad siddhi hetukā yadi nāma avagamyeta paramāṇu astitā punar 
[5,5.186ab_5,5.188cd]	tasmāt yat gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā tat tathā eva abhyupetavyam sāmānyam atha vā itarat sattā ādi sāmānyam apekṣya sarvam go tva ādi sādhāraṇa tām upaiti tasmāt asādhāraṇam akṣa gamyam vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta sāmānya rupeṇa na gṛhyate ced kim vā asti asādhāraṇa buddhiḥ atra yat vastu lokaḥ pratipadyate asmin dvidhā api tat śakti atas eva vaktum 
[5,6.1ab_5,6.3cd]	pratyakṣa ādiṣu vaktavyam śabda mātrasya lakṣaṇam adati tvaritena iha kim śāstrāt abhidhīyate sāmānya lakṣaṇam tyaktvā viśeṣasya eva lakṣaṇam na śakyam kevalam vaktum itas api asya na vācya tā yat ca uktam śabda vijñānāt arthe jñānam iti īdṛśamū aviśiṣṭam viśiṣṭasya na tad śāstrasya lakṣaṇam 
[5,6.4ab_5,6.7ab]	pravṛttiḥ vā nivṛttiḥ vā nityena kṛtakena vā puṃsām yena upadiśyeta tat śāstram abhidhīyate svarūpa kathanam yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate tad aṅga tvena tasya api śāstra tvam avagamyate bhāvanāyām samastāyām vākyāt eva upajāyate pravṛttiḥ vā nivṛttiḥ vā tat śāstram na padāt yatas aparīkṣā āmiṣeṇa api lakṣaṇāni vadan ayam 
[5,6.7cd_5,6.10cd]	na svatantra upayogi tva nirapekṣāṇi jalpati tatra yat loka vākya stham kathayet śabda lakṣaṇam vedam vyākhyātu kāmasya tat na atīva upayujyate pratyakṣa ādi upayogam tu varṇa mātra āditaḥ puras śāstra artha jñāna velāyām matvā tad lakṣaṇam kṛtam yat tu gāmānaya ityādi vākya stham śabda lakṣaṇam tasya na iha upayogaḥ asti tasmāt śāstra gatam kṛtam 
[5,6.11ab_5,6.14ab]	veśeṣaḥ ca na sāmānyam antareṇa asti kaḥ cana tasmāt tam api udāhṛtya sāmānyam lakṣayet sukham sāmānya rūpam api etad adhikārāt viśiṣyate codanā ca upadeśaḥ ca śāstram eva iti udāhṛtam yathā ca codanā śabdaḥ vaidikyām eva vartate śabda jñāna artha vijñāna śabdau śāstre tathā sthitau pratyakṣa ādi a parīkṣya tve tad antar bhāva hetukam 
[5,6.14cd_5,6.17ab]	śāstrasya api aparīkṣya tvam anayā eva dhiyā uditam tatra anumānam eva idam bauddhaiḥ vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam bhedaḥ sāṃkhya ādibhiḥ tu iṣṭaḥ na tu uktam bheda kāraṇam pūrva saṃskāra yukta antya varṇa vākya ādi kalpanā vivakṣā ādi ca dhūma ādau na asti iti etena bhinna tā yaiḥ uktā tatra vaidharmya vikalpa sama jāti tā 
[5,6.17cd_5,6.20cd]	dhūma anitya viṣāṇi ādi viśeṣāt na hi bhinna tā taila kṣaṇya parityāgaḥ yāvat na pratipādyate tāvat viśeṣa mātreṇa vadataḥ jātitā bhavet yathā iṣṭa viniyogena pratītiḥ yā api śabdataḥ na dhūma ādeḥ iti iha api vyabhicāraḥ aṅga vṛttibhiḥ hasta saṃjñā ādayaḥ ye api yad artha pratipādane bhaveyuḥ kṛta saṅketāḥ te na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ 
[5,6.21ab_5,6.24ab]	puruṣa ākṣipta tayām ca tathā eva vyabhicāritā pada vaidika vākyānām na satya vyāpitā bhavet sambandhātubhavaḥ ca ayam saḥ anyatra api vilakṣaṇaḥ etasmin puruṣa apekṣā deśa apekṣā agni dhūmayoḥ kāla ādi apekṣayā ca anyaḥ uktā ca anyaiḥ abhinnatā āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumānataḥ na ca apūrva ādi śabdānām bhedāt sarvatra bhinna tā 
[5,6.24cd_5,6.27ab]	na ca iha aśva ādi śabdebhyaḥ bhedaḥ teṣām pratīyate na ca api ajñāta sambandham padam kiñ cit prakāśakam sambandhān anubhūtyā atas na syāt ananumāna tā tulya ākāra tayā api atra śabda jñāna artha tad dhiyām agni dhūmeṣu adṛṣṭa tvāt na bhedaḥ tad nivāraṇāt pratibimbeṣu anaikāntaḥ bimbam yādṛś hi darpaṇe 
[5,6.27cd_5,6.30cd]	tādṛś mukha ādi budhyante na ca atra ananumāna tā pratyakṣatā tadā api atra tadā anyaiḥ vyabhicāritā yatra pāda ādi bambena gatānām anumīyate eka vākyāt sakṛt ca uktān na api anekasya tad kṣaṇam syāt viruddha aviruddhasya bodhāt etasya bhinnātā liṅgasya api hi tādrūpyam dṛṣṭam hetu viruddhayoḥ virodhāt na anumānam ced syāt anāgamatā api te 
[5,6.31ab_5,6.33cd]	yatra ca ekārtha tā vākye tatra syāt anumāna tā sakṛt uccarite ca asmin vivakṣā ekā eva dṛśyate yaḥ tu anirdhānam ca dhūma ādau vyabhicāritam sa liṅge api asphuṭe dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt na etena bhidyate dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānam ca dhūma ādau vyabhicāritam prasiddha tvāt dhi tatra api na dṛṣṭāntaḥ abhidhīyate 
[5,6.34ab_5,6.36cd]	anabhyaḥ te tu apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim atra pratyuktaḥ iti evam budhyante hi cirāt kva cit para uktā hetavaḥ ca atra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ śabda anumānayoḥ aikyam dhūmāt agni anumāna vat anvaya vyatirekābhyām eka pratyakṣa darśanāt sambandha pūrvaka tvāt ca pratipattiḥ itas yatas 
[5,6.37ab_5,6.39cd]	pratyakṣa anyapramāṇa tvāt tad adṛṣṭa artha bodhanāt sāmānya viṣaya tvāt ca traikālya viṣaya āśrayāt kaiḥ cit mīmāṃsakaiḥ uktaḥ bhedaḥ atra viṣaya antarāt pūrvābhyām hi aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate tatra api na āgama tvam syāt puruṣa ukte tathā as tu ced pratyayaḥ kid nimittaḥ arthe vaktṛ buddheḥ kutas nu asau 
[5,6.40ab_5,6.43ab]	na śabda arthasya sa āliṅgam na śabdaḥ asyāḥ kathan cana viśeṣaḥ gamyate tābhyām na ca etasya anumeya tā tena vaktuḥ abhiprāye pratyakṣa ādya nirūpite puruṣoktiḥ api śrotuḥ āgama tvam prapadyate na ca api ananumeya tvam āgama arthasya śakyate liṅgam hi śabdaḥ eva asya dhūmaḥ agneḥ iva kalpyate na ca api ananumeyavāt pramāṇa antara gamya tā 
[5,6.43cd_5,6.46cd]	rūpasya aśrāvaṇa tvena na hi apratyakṣata iṣyate evam sati sva yūthyāḥ na ke cit na ati prapañcinaḥ anumāna viśeṣaḥ ayam īdṛś dharmasya bodhakaḥ bhaviṣyati artha rūpam tu liṅgam dharme nirākṛtam saṃjñā anumāna tā icchā tu na duṣyet āgame api naḥ lakṣaṇena tu abhinna tvam yadi śabda anumānayoḥ veda jñāna apramāṇa tvam syāt atad lakṣaṇa tvataḥ 
[5,6.47ab_5,6.50ab]	āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyān nṛvacassu hi lakṣaṇena anumāna tvāt prāmāṇyam siddhim ṛcchati vede tu āpta nara abhāvāt sambandha anubhavāt ṛte lakṣaṇam na anumānasya iti aprāmāṇyam prasajyate nanu eka deśa satya tve tasya syāt anumāna tā veda tvāt agni hotra ādau vāyu kṣepiṣṭha vākya vat na āditya yūpe anaikāntāt tadvat vā gauṇa tā bhavet 
[5,6.50cd_5,6.53cd]	na atas pratyanumānānām evam pūrva uktayā viśā tasmāt lakṣaṇa bhedena yadi śabda pramāṇa tā samā loke ca vede ca siddhā veda pramāṇa tā tena ca āpta upadeśa tvam na syāt āgama lakṣaṇam na āptasya sambhavaḥ vede loke na asmāt pramāṇa tā purastāt varṇitam hi etat tsmāt śabdena yā matiḥ tasyāḥ svatas pramāṇa tvam na ced syāt doṣa darśanam

[5,6.57cd_5,6.60ab]	sāmarthyāt anumeya tvāt aśrute api pada antare saṃkhyā ādimān padārthaḥ ced na tāvat saḥ avyaya ādiṣu yatra api te pratīyante tatra vyakteḥ viśeṣaṇam pada antara abhidheyasya tādarthyāt ca kriyā ātmanaḥ vākya arthe api padam yatra gomada ādi prayujyate sati api atra viśeṣṭa tve siddha tvāt na eva pakṣatā 
[5,6.60cd_5,6.63ab]	tāvān eva hi tatra arthaḥ yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ bheda buddheḥ ca vaiṣamyam prakṛti pratyaya arthayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya artha svātantrya grahaṇam na ca viśeṣya pūrvikā tatra buddhiḥ ca atra viparyayaḥ atha śabdaḥ arthavat tvena pakṣaḥ kasmāt na kalpyate pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hi hetuḥ tatra prasajyate 
[5,6.63cd_5,6.66ab]	pakṣe dhūma viśeṣe ca sāmānyam hetuḥ iṣyate śabda tvam gamakam na atra go śabda tvam niṣetsyate vyaktiḥ eva viśiṣyātaḥ hetuḥ ca ekā prasajyate bhavet vyañjaka bhedāt ced na tu evam pratyayaḥ asti naḥ katham ca asya viśiṣṭa tvam na tāvat deśa kālataḥ tad pratīti viśiṣṭaḥ ced param kim anumīyate 
[5,6.66cd_5,6.69cd]	na pratyāyana śaktiḥ ca viśeṣasya anumīyate viśeṣāṇām na śaktiḥ hi sa eka deśe agni jāti vat sāmānyasya eva śakta tvam pakṣaḥ hetuḥ tat eva ca tasmāt artha viśiṣṭasya na śabdasya anumeya tā katham ca pakṣa dharma tvam śabdasya iha nirūpyate na kriyā kartṛ sambandhāt ṛte sambandhanam kva cit rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ saḥ ucyate 
[5,6.70ab_5,6.72cd]	vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tāḥ vā tatra iti tasya tāḥ deśe agnimati dhūmasya kartṛ tvam bhavanam prati kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate na ca anavagata ākāraḥ sambandhaḥ asti iti gamyate na ca asti asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhī tatpuruṣaḥ api vā tasmāt na pakṣa dharmaḥ ayam iti śakyā nirūpaṇā 
[5,6.73ab_5,6.75cd]	nivṛtte anyatra sambandhe ye api tad viṣaya ātmanā vadeyuḥ pakṣa dharma tvam śabdasya anupalabdhi vat taiḥ api etat nirūpyam tu śabdaḥ tad viṣayaḥ katham na tad deśa ādi sadbhāvaḥ nābhi mukhya ādi tasya vā tasmāt utpādayati eṣa yatas artha viṣayāḥ matim tena tad viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ iti dharma tva kalpanā

[5,6.79ab_5,6.81cd]	na ca sva rūpa mātreṇa dhūma ādeḥ pakṣa dharma tā na ca api pūrva sambandham apekṣya eṣā prasajyate dhūmavān ayam iti evam apūrvasya api jāyate pakṣa dharma matiḥ tena bhidyeta uttara lakṣaṇāt na tu atra pūrva sambandhāt adhikā pakṣa dharma tā na ca artha pratyayāt pūrvam iti anaṅgam iyam bhavet 
[5,6.82ab_5,6.84cd]	na ca dharmī gṛhītaḥ atra yena tad dharmatā bhavet parvata ādiḥ yathā deśaḥ prāc dharma tva avadhāraṇāt yaḥ ca atra kathyate dharmī prameyaḥ asya saḥ eva naḥ na ca anavadhṛte tasmin tad dharma tva avadhāraṇam prāk sa ced pakṣa dharma tvāt gṛhītaḥ kim tatas param paṣa dharma ādibhiḥ jñātaiḥ yena syāt anumānitā 
[5,6.85ab_5,6.87cd]	anvayaḥ na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvita tvam pratīyate yatra dhūmaḥ asti tatra agneḥ astitvena anvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ na tu evam yatra śabdaḥ asti tatra arthaḥ asti iti niścayaḥ na tāvat tatra deśe asau tad kāle vā avagamyate bhavet nitya vibhu tvāt ced sarva artheṣu ca tat samam

[5,6.91ab_5,6.93cd]	dvitīya ādi prayoge ca bhavet anvaya kalpanā śata kṛtvas prayukte api na ca dṛṣṭa artha dhīḥ kva cit nanu ye jñāta sambandhāḥ teṣām dṛṣṭaḥ anvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ yadi evam anvayāt pūrvam sambandhaḥ kaḥ api kalpitaḥ na aṅgam artha dhiyām eṣā bhavet anvaya kalpanā anvaya adhīna janma tvam anumānasya ca sthitam

[5,6.100ab_5,6.102cd]	padam prayujyamānam hi caturddha arthe prayujyate pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte ajñāte api vā purā tatra yat pūrva vijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate pramite ca prayukta tvāt anuvādaḥ adhikāt vinā adṛṣṭa pūrve tu ajñānam sambandha pratyayaḥ api vā sambandhaḥ na ca tasya arthaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ sa tu anya gocaraḥ 
[5,6.103ab_5,6.106ab]	parokṣe ananubhūte ca na abhidheye matiḥ bhavet parokṣaḥ ca anubhūtaḥ ca yaḥ tatra smṛtiḥ iṣyate pramite ca pravṛtta tvāt smṛteḥ na asti pramāṇa tā pariccheda phala tvāt dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate tādātvika pariccheda phala tvena pramāṇa tā pratyabhijñāna vat kasmāt smṛteḥ api na kalpyate yāvān pūrva paricchinnaḥ tāvān eva avadhāryate 
[5,6.106cd_5,6.111cd]	smṛtyā tad anusāreṇa tadā asattve asya na eva dhīḥ padam abhyadhika abhāvāt smārakāt na viśiṣyate pada ādhikyam bhavet kiñ cit tad padasya na gocaraḥ prāṇam anumānam vā yadi api syāt padāt mitiḥ vākya arthasya āgama artha tvāt doṣaḥ na āgama vādinām vākya arthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandha anubhavāt ṛte buddhiḥ utpadyate tena bhinnā asau akṣa buddhi vat vākya adhikaraṇe ca asya hetoḥ siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati sarveṣām ca paroktānām vākya buddhau asiddha tā vākyeṣu adṛṣṭeṣu api sārthakeṣu padārtha vid mātra tayā pratītim dṛṣṭvā anumāna vyatireka bhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padā bheda vicāraṇāyām 
[5,7.1ab_5,7.4ab]	kīdṛś gavayaḥ iti evam pṛṣṭaḥ nāgarikaiḥ yadi bravīti āraṇyakaḥ vākyam yathā gauḥ gavayaḥ tathā etasmin upamāna tvam prasiddham śabare punar tasya āgamā bahirbhāvāt anyathā eva upavarṇitam puruṣa pratyayena eva tatra arthaḥ sampratīyate tadīya vacana tvena tasmāt āgamaḥ eva saḥ sadṛśāt upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśa antare 
[5,7.4cd_5,7.7cd]	dhyāna ādi smṛti tulya tvāt sā pramāṇam katham bhavet deśa kāla ādi bhedena yathā anyatra viśiṣyate prameyam na evam asti atra nagara stha anusārataḥ śruta atideśa vākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ yā sa upamānam keṣān cit go sādṛśya anurañjitā pratyakṣaḥ gavayaḥ tāvat sādṛśya smṛtiḥ atra tu nanu sādṛśya yukte arthe na smṛtiḥ na indriyāt gatiḥ 
[5,7.8ab_5,7.11ab]	pūrva vākya artha vijñānāt na ādhikyam gavaye yadi smaraṇāt aviśiṣṭa tvāt saṅgateḥ na pramāṇa tā atha tu adhika tā kā cit pratyakṣa ādi vaśāt bhavet yāvat hīndriya sambandhaḥ tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam syaryamāṇasya ca aṃśasya vivedena apramāṇa tā śruta atideśa vākya tvam na ca atīva upayujyate ye api hi aśruta tad vākyāḥ teṣām api bhavati ayam

[5,7.18ab_5,7.21ab]	sādṛśyasya api vastu tvam na śakyam apabādhitum bhūyas avayava sāmānya yogaḥ jāti antarasya tat sadṛśa avayava tvam tu yatra padma dala akṣi vat tat sva avayava sāmānya bhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati evam jāti guṇa dravya kriyā śakti svadharmataḥ ekaika dvi tri sāmastya bhedāt etasya citra tā na dharmāḥ eva sādṛśyam bhūyas tāḥ vā tad āśrayā

[5,8.18ab_5,8.21ab]	vṛṣṭimat para deśa tvam nadī puravataḥ atra tu deśasya pratipadyante yat vā artha āpattiḥ eva sā jīvataḥ ca gṛha abhāvaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ atra kalpyate tad saṃvittiḥ bahirbhāvam na ca abuddhvā upajāyate agni mattā anapekṣā tu dhūmavat tā pratīyate na tad grahaṇa velāyām agni adhīnam hi kiñcana geha abhāvaḥ tu yaḥ śuddhaḥ vidyamāna tva varjitaḥ

[5,11.43cd_5,11.46cd]	devadatte api ca avyaktām śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ prakāśe avasthite bāhye na andhaḥ rūpam pratīyate phala anantaryatas ca api cakṣuḥ karaṇam iṣyate puruṣa adhīna vijñānaḥ tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ yaḥ saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandhaḥ sa ca iṣṭaḥ ced dhruvam kṛtaḥ bhinna deśa ādi adhiṣṭhānāt yathā rajju ghaṭa ādiṣu samam na asti anayoḥ kiñ cit tena asaṅgatatā svatas 
[5,12.1ab_5,12.3cd]	ādhāra ātmani viñāte sukham ādheya bodhanam tasya eva tāvat prastāvāt atha gauḥ iti atas abravīt pratyakṣe api visaṃvādaḥ yeṣām kaḥ svayam uttaram tebhyaḥ dadyāt iti jñātvā vṛddhānām matam abravīt tatra artha pratyaya dvāram kṛtam śabda nirūpaṇam yaiḥ āsatām tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate 
[5,12.4ab_5,12.6cd]	pratyakṣam na asamartham naḥ tena ca arthe avadhārite na hetuḥ balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tatas tasmāt śrotra paricchinnaḥ yadi artham gamayet na vā sarvathā tasya śabda tvam loka siddham na hīyate yadi tu artha gatau śaktiḥ na syāt asya tatas punar vastu antaram prakalpyeta vinā śabda prasiddhitaḥ 
[5,12.7ab_5,12.9cd]	agni ādīn gamayantaḥ api śabdāḥ dhūma ādayaḥ na hi na vā apratyāyaka tvāt syāt eka varṇeṣu aśabda tā na ca prāc artha vijñānāḥ chotra grāhye na śabda dhīḥ na ca artha jñānataḥ paścāt aśrautre api ca śabda tā paraspara anapekṣāḥ ca śrotra buddhyā svarūpataḥ varṇāḥ eva avagamyante na pūrva apara vastunī 
[5,12.10ab_5,12.13ab]	alpīyasā api yatnena śabdam uccaritam matiḥ yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇam vā sakalam sphuṭam pṛthak na ca upalabhyante varṇasya avayavāḥ kva cit na ca varṇeṣu anusyūtāḥ dṛśyante tantu vat paṭe teṣām anupalabdheḥ ca na jñātā liṅga saṅgatiḥ na āgamaḥ tad paraḥ ca asti na adṛṣṭe ca upamā kva cit na ca api anupapattiḥ syāt varṇasya avayavaiḥ vinā 
[5,12.13cd_5,12.16ab]	yathā anya avayavānām hi vinā api avayava antaraiḥ pratyakṣeṇa avabuddhaḥ ca varṇaḥ avayava varjitaḥ kim na syāt vyoma vat ca atra liṅgam tat rahitā matiḥ tadvat ca asya ekabuddhi tvāt deśa bhede api abhinnatā nanu bheda matiḥ na syāt tava api eka tva dhīḥ kutas sāmānyeṣu mama ekā dhīḥ tad vyaktiṣu ca bheda dhīḥ 
[5,12.16cd_5,12.19ab]	na hi iṣṭam bheda mātram hi na syāt eka tva dhīḥ yatas vyakteḥ tāvat na sāmānyam bhinna rūpam pratīyate varṇeṣu anyatra śabda tvāt na anyat ced varṇaḥ eva saḥ saḥ eva iti matiḥ na api sādṛśyam na ca tat kva cit vinā avayava sāmānyāt varṇeṣu avayavāḥ na ca pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt ca na anya apohaḥ api yujyate 
[5,12.19cd_5,12.22cd]	vācakaḥ ca atra liṅgam vā na tadānīm pratīyate gakāra ādiṣu sāmānyam śabda tvam kalpyate yathā go tvam ca śābaleya ādau tathā etat kim na kalpyate śābaleyaga kāra dīn niṣpannān vyakti rūpataḥ sāmānya dhīḥ na gṛhṇāti iti atas jātiḥ api iṣyate na tu druta ādi bhede api niṣpannā sampratīyate gavyakti antara vyāvṛttā gavyaktiḥ aparā sphuṭā

[5,12.66ab_5,12.69ab]	anārabdhe ca go śabde go śabda tvam katham bhavet varṇa sāmānya vat ca api na tad kalpanam arhati varṇa ātmanām abhedāt ca siddhā sāmānya dhīḥ api samudāyaḥ api tebhyaḥ asyaḥ vā araṇīyaḥ anayā diśā abheda samudāyaḥ tu teṣām dharmaḥ na duṣyati teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam artha pratyāyanam prati yāvantaḥ yādṛśaḥ ye ca yad artha pratipādane 
[5,12.69cd_5,12.72ab]	varṇāḥ prajñāta sāmarthyāḥ te tathiva avabodhakāḥ teṣām tu guṇa bhūtānām artha pratyāyanam prati sāhityam eka kartṛ ādi kramaḥ ca api vivakṣitaḥ kartrā eka tve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam prayuñjānasya yat pūrvam vṛddhebhyaḥ krama darśanam yaugapadyam tu aśakya tvāt na eva teṣām iha āśritam 
[5,12.72cd_5,12.75ab]	kartṛ bhedaḥ ca tatra syāt na ca evam dṛśyate abhidhā yugapad dṛśya sāmarthyāḥ na eva śaktāḥ krame yathā bhāvāḥ tathā krame śaktāḥ yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ca pūrṇamāsa ādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatya kāriṇaḥ abhyāsānām ca loke api svādhyāya grahaṇa ādiṣu sādhana ādi trayāṇām ca vyāpārasya eka kālatā

[5,12.94ab_5,12.97ab]	sadbhāva vyatirekau ca tathā avayava varjanam tava adhikam bhavet tasmāt yatnaḥ asau artha buddhiṣu na anyathā anupapattiḥ ca bhavet artha matim prati tat eva asyāḥ nimittam syāt jāyate yat anantaram sā ca varṇa dvaya jñāne atīte antya jñānataḥ parā bhavati iti īdṛś eva asyāḥ nimittam avakalpate vinā saṃskāra kalpena tad anantara vṛttitaḥ 
[5,12.97cd_5,12.100cd]	kṛta anugraha sāmarthyaḥ varṇaḥ antyaḥ pratipādakaḥ eṣaḥ eva tu saṃskāraḥ iti ke cit pracakṣate adṛṣṭa kalpanā atītam tāvat mātram hi dṛśyate atha vā vāsanā eva astu saṃskāraḥ sarve eva hi dṛḍha jñāna gṛhīte arthe saṃskāraḥ asti iti manvate tasya artha buddhi hetu tve visaṃvādaḥ asya nirṇaye tad bhāva bhāvitā hetuḥ anyatra iva pratīyate

[5,12.107ab_5,12.109cd]	varṇānām yaugapadyena yadi ca avaśyam arthitā nitya tvāt sarvadā tat syāt na tu kāraṇa tā tathā ittham krama gṛhītānām yugapad yā atha vā parā sthitiḥ sā kāraṇam tu syāt nityam arthadhiyam prati yat vā pratyakṣatas pūrvam krama jñāneṣu yat param samasta varṇa vijñānam tad artha jñāna kāraṇam

[5,12.113ab_5,12.116ab]	sarveṣu ca evam artheṣu mānasam sarva vādinām iṣṭam samuccaya jñānam krama jñāneṣu satsu api na ced tadā abhyupeyeta krama dṛṣṭeṣu na eva hi śata ādi rūpam jāyeta tat samuccaya darśanam tena śrotram anobhyām syāt kramāt varṇeṣu yadi api pūrva jñānam parastāt tu yugapad smaraṇam bhavet tad ārūḍhāḥ tatas varṇāḥ na dūre artha avabodhanāt

[5,12.119cd_5,12.122ab]	varṇa traya parityāge buddhiḥ na anyatra jāyate gauḥ iti ekam ati tvam tu na eva asmābhiḥ nivāryate tad grāhya ekārthatābhyām ca śabde syāt eka tā matiḥ śaidhyāt alpa antara tvāt ca go śabde sā abhavet api deva datta ādi śabdeṣu sphuṭaḥ bhedaḥ pratīyate na gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti evam grantha sambandhanam bhavet

[5,14.53ab_5,14.55cd]	aga vya śvātiḥ ekaḥ syāt anaśvaḥ ca gavādhikaḥ śeṣam hasti ādi apohyam tu dvayoḥ api na bhidyate tatra eka bhedāt bhedaḥ astu bahu abhedāt abhinnatā bhūyasām syāt sadharma tvam iti abhedaḥ prasajyate gauḥ ca hasti ādi apohena na aśva rūpāt viśeṣyate karoti tat apoham ced aikarūpyam virudhyate

[5,14.59cd_5,14.62cd]	tatra ekasmin bhavet piṇḍe ananta jāti samanvayaḥ tatas gauḥ iti sāmānyam vācyam ekam na sidhyati jāti antara matiḥ ca eṣu bhavet jāti antareṣu iva samudāya ātmanā na api bhavet eṣām apohyatā samudāyaḥ hi na ekena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate na api eka deśa tā teṣām asti na api eka kāla tā vyatiriktaḥ ca saṅghātaḥ teṣām kaḥ cit na vidyate 
[5,14.63ab_5,14.66ab]	yadi tu avyatiriktaḥ syāt ānanyam tat avasthitam yadi sāmānya rūpeṇa te apohyante na vastu tā katham vā vastu apohyeta na abhāvaḥ bhāvam ṛcchati apohyamāne ca abhāve bhāvaḥ eva avaśiṣyate apohya bheda kḷptiḥ ca na abhāva abhedataḥ bhavet tad bhedaḥ apoha bhedāt ced prāptam anyonya saṃśrayam go sāmāni asya bhinna tvāt agauḥ iti eṣa bhidyate

[5,14.79ab_5,14.81cd]	pūrva uktena prabandhena na anumā api atra vidyate sambandha anubhāvaḥ api asya tena na eva upapadyate nivṛtti vācinaḥ śabdāḥ na prasiddhāḥ ca yān prati teṣām agoḥ asiddha tvāt na sāmānya nirākriyā ago śabda abhidheya tvam gamyatām ca katham punar na dṛṣṭaḥ yatra go śabdaḥ sambandha anubha vakṣaṇe

[5,14.169ab_5,14.171cd]	sādhya hīnaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi api tasya hi varttate apohavati eva tam yadi api na budhyate atha anya apoha nirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddha sādhanam apoha rūpam api etat vastu iti eva hi gamyate atha apoha nimitta asya vṛttiḥ arthe niṣidhyate vyatireka aṅgateṣṭa tvāt punar prāk pakṣa bādhanam 
[5,14.172ab_5,14.176cd]	anumāne tathā ca etat iti anaikāntikaḥ bhavet sandeha bādha jātena pratyakṣeṇa api cetasā viruddha tā ca hetoḥ syāt śabdaḥ śrotra ādi vat yatas ātma antaḥ karaṇa ākāśaiḥ sva vāci tvam jahāti vāḥ vidhi rūpa pravṛttiḥ vā śabdaḥ apohena varttate anumāna aṅga bhūta tvāt yathā eva pratiṣedhakaḥ jātim vā na bravīti eṣa vyaktim vā tad viśeṣitām pramāyām aṅga bhūta tvāt tvac śrotra ādi yathā eva ca evam sādhana mārgeṇa vācya avācya nirūpaṇā na avātiṣṭhate iti atra kathyate loka vartmanā 
[5,15.1ab_5,15.4ab]	sāsnādibhiḥ viśiṣṭa tvam ākṛteḥ ucyate katham yadā avayavi sambandhi go tvam na avayave sthitam eka avayavi sambandhaḥ teṣām go tvena vidyate tena asādhāraṇa tvāt te syuḥ go tvasya upalakṣaṇam piṇḍe sattā ādi jātīnām bahvīnām samaveta tā tābhyaḥ viśiṣyate go tvam sāsnādibhiḥ asaṃśayam na ca ete vyañjakāḥ tasya guṇavat vā viśeṣaṇam 
[5,15.4cd_5,15.7ab]	tathā hi na agṛhīteṣu teṣu syāt go tva bodhanam teṣām ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punar grahaṇa kalpanā tathā sati anavasthā syāt na syāt go tva avadhāraṇam sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavet matiḥ go tve na ca eṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhi sambhavaḥ tasmāt sadbhāva mātreṇa mahat tva ādau yathā eva dhīḥ 
[5,15.7cd_5,15.10cd]	kriyate avayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jāti guṇa ādiṣu yadi evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kim sā na jāyate tad deśa vyatirekeṇa grāhyam yena na vidyate gṛhyamāṇe tu go tva ādau na antarīyaka hetukaḥ sāsnādeḥ kasya cit bodhaḥ tad deśa tvena jāyate tad anatyanta bhedāt vā tad viśiṣṭa iti kīrtyate bādhaḥ para anumānasya na pratyakṣā iti bodhyate

[5,16.22ab_5,16.24cd]	vaktuḥ anyaḥ hi sambandhaḥ buddhau śrotuḥ tathā aparaḥ śrotuḥ kartum ca sambandham vaktā kam pratipadyatām pūrva dṛṣṭaḥ hi yaḥ tena śrotuḥ na eva karoti tam yam karoti navam saḥ api na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ sarvathā śrotṛ siddhiḥ ced asiddham na itaraḥ vadet ghaṭa ādau api tulyam ced na sāmānya prasiddhitaḥ

[5,17.22cd_5,17.26cd]	ānantaryam upetya eva te svābhāvika vādinaḥ svargasya amuṣmika tvam tu ṣaṣṭha ādye sthāpayiṣyate paśu ādeḥ niyama abhāvaḥ yoga siddhiḥ iti iha tu yadā kadā cit bhavat etat iṣyate phalam hi paśu ādi na sāmparāyikam tathā sthitasya eva hi tasya sādhanam vidhīyate yaḥ api bhṛśam tvarā anvitaḥ sādhāraṇam yat tu palam bahūnām svabhāvataḥ tādṛśam eva ceṣṭam sarvasya vā aasat na tayā eva kāmyam vṛṣṭi ādi tat ca aihikam eva yuktam kamipadam aviśiṣṭam yadi api śrūyate vā bhavati phala viśeṣī na anyathā kāmyate hi phalati yadi ni sarva tat kadā cit tadā eva dhruvam aparam abhuktam karma śāstrī yamāḥ te 
[5,18.1ab_5,18.3cd]	sākṣāt yadi api sambandhaḥ na ātmanaḥ yajña sādhanaiḥ tathā api lakṣaṇa āvṛttyā śarīra dvārakaḥ bhavet pratyakṣa tvam ca deha stham bhāktam ātmani kalpitam ātmanaḥ svarga yānam vā śarīrasya upacaryyate nairātmyena atra ca ākṣiptāḥ sarvāḥ eva hi codanāḥ sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ tad uktaḥ na hi siddhyati 
[5,18.4ab_5,18.7ab]	tāḥ hi kartuḥ phalena āhuḥ sambandham kvāpi janmani na ca vijñāna mātra tve bhoktṛ kartṛ tva sambhavaḥ śarīra vinipātāt ca param na anyat yat ā iṣyate adatta phalaiṣṭi ādau tadā tat vacanam mṛṣā tasmāt veda pramāṇa artham ātmā atra pratipādyate yadi api prakṛtam vākyam vyākhyāyeta artha vādataḥ śarīra indriya buddhibhyaḥ vyatirikta tvam ātmanaḥ 
[5,18.7cd_5,18.10ab]	nitya tvam ca iṣyate śeṣam śarīra ādi vinaśyate nityaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve pratipannaḥ api san yadā na karma phala sambandham bhoga kāle avabudhyate mayā yat tu kṛtam karma tasya idam bhujyate phalam śubha aśubham mayā eva iti tadā kaḥ asya rasaḥ bhavet aprāmṛśyamāne hi sva karma pratyaye phale 
[5,18.10cd_5,18.13ab]	na viśeṣaḥ bhavet kaḥ cit sva para ātmā upabhogayoḥ kurvan api aśubham karma tena evam cintayet naraḥ na smariṣyāmi bhoge aham iti na etat vivarjayet tatra nitya tva pakṣe api kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau phalatas tulya rūpau ced vṛthā tad pratipādanam na eṣa doṣaḥ na bhoge hi smṛtiḥ naḥ upayujyate 
[5,18.13cd_5,18.16ab]	na pravṛtiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā bhoga kāle smṛteḥ bhavet tad aṅgam yaḥ parāmarśaḥ tat astitvam ca mṛgyate prāk pravṛtteḥ tu saḥ asti eva viduṣām śāstrataḥ sphuṭaḥ paścāt api ca śāstra jñāḥ vimṛśanti eva ke cana teṣām eva adhikāraḥ ca mā bhūt aviduṣām tu saḥ parāmarśaḥ ca sarvatra na asti sarva pramāṇakaḥ

[5,18.23ab_5,18.25cd]	syātām atyanta nāśe asya kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau na tu avasthā antara prāptau loke bāla yuva ādi vat avasthā antara bhāvyetat phalam mama śubha aśubham iti jñātvā anutiṣṭhan ca vijahat ceṣṭate janaḥ anavasthā antara prāptiḥ dṛśyate na ca kasya cit anucchedāt tu na anya tvam bhoktuḥ lokaḥ avagacchati

[5,18.120ab_5,18.122cd]	santānaḥ na ca tat grāhyaḥ dvairūpyasya asambhavāt jñātavān na hi asau pūrvam avastu tvāt na vā adhunā sāmānyam na ca kiñ cit te jñātṛ pūrva aparakṣaṇe sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñā ced na syāt asadṛśeṣu sā gām aham jñātavān pūrvam aśvam jānāmi aham punar atha jñātṛ tva sāmānyam tat syāt deha antareṣu api 
[5,18.123ab_5,18.125cd]	tatra sarveṇa vijñāte bhavet aham iti smṛtiḥ eka santāna je ca api saḥ iti syāt kṣaṇe matiḥ yathā deha antara jñāne ghaṭa ādau vā bahis sthite jñātari pratyabhijñām ca vāsanā kartum arhati na ātasmin saḥ iti jñānam na hi asau bhrānti kāraṇam na ca aham pratyayaḥ bhrāntiḥ iṣṭaḥ bādhaka varjanāt 
[5,18.126ab_5,18.128cd]	jñātuḥ anyaḥ ca viṣayaḥ tasya na syāt svabhāvataḥ aham pratyaya vijñeyaḥ jñātāḥ naḥ sarvadā eva hi guruḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśaḥ vā aham iti dehe api yā matiḥ bhrāntiḥ sā bheda rūpam hi guru me tat iti iṣyate idam mama īdṛśam cakṣuḥ manaḥ me bhrāntam iti api indriyeṣu api bhedena vyavahāraḥ ca dṛśyate 
[5,18.129ab_5,18.131cd]	ajñātṛ tvasya siddha tvāt virodhāt bhedavatī api pratyāsatti nimittaḥ tu syāt abheda matiḥ bhramaḥ mama ātmā iti mati bheda vyapadeśena yātmanaḥ tatra avasthā ātmanā bhedam jñānasya āśritya kalpanā mama iti etasya mukhya arthaḥ na ātmanaḥ anyaḥ pratīyate tena asau bheda hetuḥ syāt bhedaḥ ca jñāna hetukaḥ 
[5,18.132ab_5,18.134cd]	ye ca iha ājñāta nānātvāḥ teṣām deheṣu aham matiḥ tatra api ātma abhimānena iti ahambuddhiḥ dhruva ātmani ye tu vijñāta nānātvāḥ te deheṣu anahaṃkṛtāḥ jānāmi aham iti idam tu jñānam na eva nivarttate tad nivṛttau na teṣām syāt dhyānam śiṣya upadeśane pravṛttiḥ dṛśyate sā ca tena ātmā taiḥ pratīyate 
[5,18.135ab_5,18.138ab]	śāstrāt avardha vijñāte yadi aham jñātavān iti na avagacchet tatas sarvaḥ pravarteta āditas punar tena asmāt pratyabhijñānāt sarva loka avadhāritāt nairātmya vāda bādhaḥ syāt ete ca pratihetavaḥ hyastana āhamm atigrāhyaḥ jñātādya api anuvarttate ahaṃpratyaya gamya tvāt id ānīnta ba uddhṛ vat eṣa vā hyas bhavet jñātā jñātṛ tvāt tat eva vā 
[5,18.138cd_5,18.141cd]	hyastana jñātṛ vat teṣām pratyayānām ca sādhya tā eka santāna sambandhi jñātra hampratyaya tvataḥ hyastanāt yatanāḥ save tulya arthaḥ ca eka buddhi vat vedāt eva ātmanā astitvam yaḥ nāma pratipadyate virodham vā ātmanā brūyāt tam prati brāhmaṇa abhidhā anyathā anupapatteḥ ca vidhinā ātmani apekṣite astitvat yotanāt etaiḥ artha ākṣipta samarthanam 
[5,18.142ab_5,18.145ab]	śāntāyām vācya śaktāyām ātmā kena prakāśyate ātmanā eva prakāśyaḥ ayam ātmā jyotiḥ iti īritam agrāhya iti sāmānyāt sarveṇa iti pratīyate ātma jyotiṣṭvavacanāt paraiḥ iti avatiṣṭhate arthāt eva artha buddhiḥ yā sā śuddhā eva upamā ucyate sādṛśya bodhanam śabdaiḥ upamāna āgamau punar ātma jñāna ā inābhūta dṛṣṭa ceṣṭā nirūpaṇāt 
[5,18.145cd_5,18.148cd]	pareṣām ātma vijñānam anumānāt udāhṛtam sadasat nāśya nāśa ātma parikīrtanam ūḍhayā coditaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ ayam iti siddhāntam abravīt avināśī svarūpeṇa puruṣaḥ yā tu nāśitā mātrāṇām sā adhikārāṇām bhūta ādīnām asaṃjñitā iti āha na asti kya nirākariṣṇuḥ ātma astitām bhāṣya kṛt atra yuktyā dṛḍha tvam etat viṣayaḥ ca bodhaḥ prayāti vedānta niṣevaṇena 
[6.1ab_6.3cd]	yadi anitya tva pakṣe api śabdāt arthaḥ avagamyate anādiḥ vyavahāraḥ ca nitya tvam kim nu sādhyate satyam icchanti te api evam nyāyaḥ tatra parīkṣyate na para abhyupagatya eva prāmāṇyam avatiṣṭhate yadā hi kṣaṇikaḥ śabdaḥ na śaktaḥ artha avadhāraṇe yuktyā avadhāryate tatra nirmalā veda dhīḥ bhavet 
[6.4ab_6.6cd]	nirmūlaiḥ api vijñānaiḥ dṛṣṭa artheṣu bhavet gatiḥ śruti mātra āśraya tvāt tu dharmaḥ dauḥsthityam āśritaḥ anādi vyavahāra tvam ādimat vastu saṃśrayam pratyākhyeyam ghaṭa tva ādi jātau vyakti bhramaḥ hi saḥ sthite kūṭastha nitya tve vyavahārasya nityatā kūṭasthena vinā etena na tasya ālambanam bhavet 
[6.7ab_6.10ab]	prasiddha tvāt ṛte sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ hi na iṣyate tasmāt veda pramāṇa artham nitya tvam iha sādhyate paraspara āvinā abhāvāt anitya kṛtaka tvayoḥ kāraṇam dvaya siddhi artham kiñ cit kasya cit ucyate nānā deśau agamya tvāt yugapad tulya buddhibhiḥ asmābhiḥ kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ bhavet akṣara lekhya vat yaugapadya upalambhāt vā bhedaḥ bhedāt ca kārya tā 
[6.10cd_6.13cd]	avibhu tve hi yugapanna ekaḥ nānā avagamyate kārtyena ca avagamya tvāt eka deśe ghaṭa ādi vat śabdasya avibhūtā tasmāt anya tā asya mukha antare ekaḥ san eka deśa sthaḥ yadā ekena prayujyate tadā vaktṛ antare na syāt eka vaktṛ mukha ādi vat kāryatve syāt kriyā bhedāt phala bhedaḥ pratikriyam tena eka buddhiḥ sādṛśyāt sphuṭe anya tve avakalpate 
[6.14ab_6.16cd]	nitya tve tu ekabuddheḥ syāt na kiñ cit bhrānti kāraṇam kāmam deśāḥ iti nyāyāt tat ca eka tvam viruddhyate na ca vyañjaka bhedena deśa bheda upalambhanam pradīpaiḥ bhinna deśa sthaiḥ na bhinnaḥ vyajyate ghaṭaḥ vyomān avayavam ca eṣām dhvanīnām āśrayaḥ matam sa vyaṅgyānām atas sarvaiḥ vyaktiḥ ekatra te bhavet 
[6.17ab_6.20ab]	vastu antara vikārya tvāt smṛti sādṛśya sādhitāt ikāra ādeḥ anitya tvam dadhi kṣīra guḍa ādi vat hetu vṛddhi anusāri tvāt kārya tā asya ghaṭa ādi vat na hi dīpa sahasre api vyañjake varddhate ghaṭaḥ anaikāntika tā tāvat hetūnām iha kathyate prayatna anantarā dṛṣṭiḥ nitye api na viruddhyate tasmāt tatra eva dṛṣṭa tvāt anyatra adṛṣṭa kalpanā

[6.23cd_6.26cd]	tau ca dvau api anāśi tvāt iṣṭa avakṛtakau api āhuḥ svabhāva siddham hi te vināśam ahetukam hetuḥ yasya vināśaḥ api tasya dṛṣṭaḥ aṅkura ādi vat vināśasya vināśaḥ tu na asti tasmāt akṛtrimaḥ bhavati hi agni sambandhāt kāṣṭāt aṅgāra santatiḥ mudgara ādi hatāt ca api kapālam jāyatte ghaṭāt svābhāvikaḥ vināśaḥ tu jāta mātra pratiṣṭitaḥ 
[6.27ab_6.30ab]	sūkṣmaḥ sadṛśa santāna dṛtteḥ anupalakṣitaḥ yadā vilakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ patet sadṛśa santatau vilakṣaṇena kāryeṇa sthūlaḥ abhivyajyate tadā tena asadṛśa santānaḥ hetoḥ san jāyate yatas tena eva akriyamāṇaḥ api nāśaḥ abhivyajyate sphūṭaḥ sa mudgara prahāra ādi prayatna anantarīyakaḥ yasmāt akṛtakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hetuḥ syāt vyabhicāryataḥ 
[6.30cd_6.33cd]	ākāśam api nityam sat yadā bhūmi jala āvṛtam vyajyate tad apohena sva nana utsecana ādibhiḥ prayatna anantaram jñānam tadā tatra api dṛśyate tena anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ yat uktam tatra darśanāt atha sthagitam api etat asti eva iti anumīyate tirohita anabhivyakteḥ śabda buddhi prabandhavat śabdasya eva anavasthānāt iti hetum vadet yadi 
[6.34ab_6.37ab]	asthānāt iti ayam hetuḥ tadā anaikāntikaḥ bhavet ākāśa dhī prabandhaḥ hi tadā tasmin na tiṣṭati tirohita anabhivyakteḥ śabda buddhi prabandhavat śabdasya eva anavasthanāt iti hetum vadet yadi asiddhaḥ eva vaktavyaḥ tatas abhivyakti vādinā tad vyāpāra kṛta tve api vyaṅgyaiḥ mūla udaka ādibhiḥ kutaka tve api teṣām hi na utpattiḥ khanana ādinā 
[6.37cd_6.40ab]	na ca āt cāraṇataḥ anyā asti śabdasya utpādikā kriyā nibandharyasatī iti evam viśiṣṭe api tathā eva naḥ abandhāḥ syuḥ yat iteṣām abodhaḥ hetu abhāvataḥ vyañjaka abhāvataḥ śabde api abodhaḥ badhira ādi vat tasya eva vā nibandhṛ tve bhavet dhetoḥ asiddha tā atha pūrva apara asattvam hituḥ tatra api asiddha tā 
[6.40cd_6.43ab]	san eva sādhāna abhāvāt śabdaḥ na eva upalabhyate kṣaṇikam sādhanam ca asya buddhiḥ api anuvartate megha andhakāra śarvaryā vidyut janita dṛṣṭi vat yathā ghaṭa ādeḥ dīpa ādiḥ abhivyañjakaḥ iṣyate cakṣuṣaḥ anugrahāt evam dhvaniḥ syāt śrītra saṃskṛteḥ na ca paryanuyogaḥ atra kena ākāreṇa saṃskṛtiḥ 
[6.43cd_6.46ab]	utpattau api tulya tvāt śaktiḥ tatra api atīndriyā nityam kārya anumeyā ca śaktiḥ kim anuyujyate tad bhāva bhāvitā mātram pramāṇam tatra gamyate atas atīndriyayā evete śaktyā śaktim atīndriyām indriyasya ādadhānāḥ syuḥ śabda abhivyakti hetavaḥ vyañjakaḥ na anya jātiḥ ced śrotram śabdasya te katham 
[6.46cd_6.49ab]	pārthivānām ghaṭa ādīnām pradopādiḥ ca taijasaḥ ātma ādi samprayoge ca kāryaiḥ syāt tulya jāti tā jātiḥ yā kā cit iṣṭā ced sā naḥ atra api bhaviṣyati upalabdhi nimittāt ca na anyat vyañjakam ucyate tasmāt yathā upalabdha tvāt sa jāti vyañjakaḥ bhavet tathā tad avinā abhāvāt vijātīyaḥ bhaviṣyati 
[6.49cd_6.52cd]	vāyavīya anabhijña tvāt tālu ādi stha abhimānataḥ anabhivyañjaka tva artham āha uparatayoḥ api vāyavīradhiyā eva uktam na nūnam iti ca uttaram abhighāta vacaḥ taḥ prāk evam gūḍha dhiyau ubhau yadi śabdam iti iha api tredhā abhivyakti sambhavaḥ sā hi syāt śabda saṃskārāt indriyasya ubhayasya vā tatra sarvaiḥ pratīyeta śabdaḥ saṃskriyate yadi 
[6.53ab_6.56ab]	nirbhāgasya vibhoḥ na syāt eka deśe hi saṃskriyā na ca asya ādhāra bhedena saṃskāra niyamaḥ bhavet yatas śabdaḥ nirādhāraḥ vyoma ātma ādi vat eva ca atha api ākāśam ādhāraḥ tatra anavayave asati na syāt pradeśa saṃskāraḥ kṛtsna śabda mateḥ api na hi sāmastya rūpeṇa yāvat vyoma vyavasthitaḥ śaktyate sakalaḥ boddhum eka deśena saṃskṛtaḥ 
[6.56cd_6.59ab]	ākāśa śrotra pakṣe ca vibhu tvāt prāpti tulya tā dūra bhāve api śabdānām iti jñānam prasajyate śrotrasya ca evam eka tvam sarva prāṇabhṛtām bhavet tena eka śruti velāyām śṛṇuyuḥ sarve eva te tasya anavayava tvāt ca na dharma adharma saṃskṛtaḥ nabhaḥ deśaḥ bhavet śrotram vyavasthā dvaya siddhayate 
[6.59cd_6.62ab]	vaiśeṣika ādi siddhānteṣu evam tāvat prasajyate kāpile api vibhu tvena śrotra ādeḥ iyam eva diś sakṛt ca saṃskṛtam śrotram sarva śabdān prabodhayet ghaṭāya unmīlitam cakṣuḥ paṭam na hi na budhyate etat eva prasaṅktavyam viṣayasya api saṃskṛtau samāna deśa varti tvāt saṃskāraḥ api aviśeṣatas 
[6.62cd_6.65ab]	sthira vāyu apanītyā ca saṃskāraḥ asya bhavan bhavet dṛṣṭam vā āvaraṇa apāye tad deśa anya upalambhanam saṃskṛta asaṃskṛta tve ca śabda eka tve na siddhi atas eka avasthā abhyupetaḥ vā sarvaiḥ jñāyeta vā na vā pratyeka abhihitāḥ doṣāḥ syuḥ dvayoḥ api saṃskṛtau tena prādeśikam jñānam na kṛta tvāt vinā bhavet 
[6.65cd_6.68ab]	uttaram śrotra saṃskārāt bhāṣya kāreṇa varṇitam tad bhedāt śruti bhedaḥ ca pratiśrotṛ vyavasthitaḥ na avaśyam śrotram ākāśam asmābhiḥ ca abhyupeyate na ca anavayavam vyoma jaina sāṃkhya niṣedhataḥ tena ākāśa eka deśaḥ vā yat vā vastu antaram bhavet kārya arthāpatti gamyam naḥ śrotram pratinaram sthiram 
[6.68cd_6.71ab]	yadi api vyāpi ca ekam ca tathā api dhvani saṃskṛtiḥ adhiṣṭhāneṣu sā yasya tat śabdam pratipatsyate atha api indriya saṃskāraḥ saḥ api adhiṣṭhāna deśataḥ śabdam na śroṣyati śrotram tena asaṃskṛta śaṣkuli aprāpta karṇa deśa tvāt dhvaneḥ na śrotra saṃskriyā atas adhiṣṭhāna bhedena saṃskāra niyama sthitiḥ 
[6.71cd_6.74cd]	nanu ekasmin adhiṣṭhāne labdha saṃskāram indriyam bodhakam sarva deheṣu syāt eka indriya vādinaḥ puṃsā deha pradeśeṣu vijñāna utpattiḥ iṣyate tena pradhāna vaideśyāt viguṇā sā tu saṃskṛtiḥ niṣpradeśaḥ api ca ātmā naḥ kārtsnyena ca vidan api śarīraḥ eva gṛhṇāti iti evam ukte na dṛṣyati eka tve api yathā ākāśam dravyaiḥ sa avayavaiḥ pṛthak 
[6.75ab_6.78ab]	saṃsarga bhedam labhate saṃskāra āsaṃskṛtaḥ tathā vyomnaḥ anavayava vyāpti sadbhāve api bhuviṣṭhitān dvi āśraya tvam na saṃsargaḥ ghaṭa ādīn anurudhyate bādhirya ādi vyavasthānam anena eva ca hetunā tat eva abhogyam anyasya dharma adharma vaśīkṛtam yathā tatra vasan eva svāmi tvāt avaropitaḥ na bhogam labhate tadvat badhiraḥ anyatra śṛṇvati 
[6.78cd_6.81cd]	śrotra śabda āśrayāṇām ca na nāma avayavāḥ svayam na ca eka deśa vṛtti tvam tathā api etat na duṣyati vyañjakānām hi vāyūnām bhinna avayava deśa tā jāti bhedaḥ ca tena eva saṃskāraḥ vyavatiṣṭhate anya artham preritaḥ vāyuḥ yathā anyam na karotivaḥ tathā anya varṇam saṃskāra śaktaḥ na anyam kariṣyati anyaiḥ tālu ādi saṃyogaiḥ varṇaḥ na anyaḥ yathā eva te 
[6.82ab_6.84cd]	tathā dhvani antarākṣepaḥ na dhvani antara sāribhiḥ tasmāt utpatti abhivyaktyoḥ kārya arthāpattitaḥ samaḥ sāmarthya bhedaḥ sarvatra syāt prayatna vivakṣayoḥ viṣayasya api saṃskāre tena ekasya eva saṃskṛtiḥ naraiḥ sāmarthya bhedāt ca na sarvaiḥ avagamyate yathā eva utpadyamānaḥ ayam na sarvaiḥ avagamyate 
[6.85ab_6.87cd]	diś deśa ādi vibhāgena sarvān prati bhavan api tathā eva yad samīpa sthaiḥ nādaiḥ syāt yasya saṃskṛtiḥ taiḥ eva śrūyate śabdaḥ na dūra sthaiḥ kathan cana dvaya saṃskāra pakṣe tu mṛṣā doṣa dvaye vacaḥ yena anyatara vaikalyāt sarvaiḥ sarvaḥ na gṛhyate sarva loka prasiddhām ca vivakṣā nusṛtām śrutim 
[6.88ab_6.90cd]	anugacchadibhiḥ ekāntāt kāryaḥ mārgaḥ parokṣakaiḥ tatra ye tāvat icchanti prāk saṃyoga vibhāgataḥ śabdaḥ utpadyate tasmāt anyaḥ tad sadṛśaḥ punar tad anantara deśe anyaḥ tādṛś anyaḥ tatas paraḥ vīcī taraṅga vṛttyā evam antyaḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyate adṛṣṭa kalpanā tasmin pakṣe bahvī prasajyate 
[6.91ab_6.94ab]	śabda bhede na tāvat naḥ prajñā bhedaḥ pravarttate ārambhaka tvam śabdasya niṣkriyasya apramāṇakam deśa antara gatam kārya na amūrtasya abhighnataḥ deśeyattā nimittam ca na ārambha niyamam prati na ca diś niyame hetuḥ anuvāta gateḥ tathā sadṛśam vā sajātim vā karoti iti ca duṣkaram ārambha sarva dikka tve na ca hetuḥ pratīyate 
[6.94cd_6.97ab]	niranvayaiḥ vinaśyadbhiḥ na ca atyanta asatām kriyā jñāna santāna vat ca eṣām santānaḥ na avakalpate vegavatsa kriya tvābhyām taraṅgāṇām tu yujyate kārya deśa antara ārambhaḥ yāvat vegam ca tad kriyā ārambha pratibandhaḥ asya na ca kuḍya ādibhibhaṃvet na hi asūrttasya sadbhāvaḥ sūrta madhye vihanyate 
[6.97cd_6.100ab]	na ca kuḍya ādibhiḥ vyoma nāśyate sāryate api vā na tirodhīyate tasmāt kuḍya madhye api tat dhruvam ākāśam tatra na syāt ced kuḍya sthānam virudhyate tat madhya avayavānām ca na hi tiṣṭhati te ghane atha āvṛtya ātmaka dravya saṃyoga rahitam nabhaḥ śabda utpādam bibharti iti tatra nyāyaḥ na kaḥ cana 
[6.100cd_6.103cd]	anyathā api upapanna tvāt na artha apattyā etat iṣyate na pramāṇa antaram ca iyam pramāṇa dvaya vādinām sambandha anupalabdheḥ ca na anumānena kalpanā brūyāt sāmānya dṛṣṭam ced bhavet dhetoḥ viruddha tā sajātīya karaḥ śabdaḥ guṇa tvāt ca indriya ādi vat aśabda ārambhakaḥ tadvat syāt adeśa antare tathā yatra hi avayavāḥ deśe paṭa ādīnām vyavasthitāḥ 
[6.104ab_6.107ab]	tatra eva tad guṇāḥ sarve tad ā ārabdhaḥ avayavi api tad guṇāḥ ca api tad deśāḥ tena eṣām eka deśa tā tadvat ādyāḥ pṛthak deśāḥ śabdāḥ sarve bhavanti hi śabdam na ārabhate śabdaḥ śabda tvāt antya śabda vat evam vibhāga saṃyogau tad bhāvāt antya yoga vat jainakāpila nirdiṣṭam śabda śrotra ādi sarpaṇam sādhīyaḥ asmāt tat api atra yuktyā na eva avatiṣṭhate 
[6.107cd_6.110ab]	śabdasya āgamanam tāvat adṛṣṭam parikalpitam mūrti sparśa ādimattvam ca teṣām abhibhavaḥ satām tvac agrāhya tvam anye ca bhāgāḥ sūkṣmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām adṛśyamānānām katham ca racanā kramaḥ kīdṛśāt racanā bhedāt varṇa bhedaḥ ca jāyate drava tvena vinā ca eṣām saṃśleṣaḥ kathyate katham 
[6.110cd_6.113ab]	āgacchatām ca viśleṣaḥ na bhavet vāyunā katham laghavaḥ avayavāḥ hi ete nibaddhā na ca kena cit vṛkṣa ādi abhihatānām ca viśleṣaḥ loṣṭa vat bhavet eka śrotra praveśe ca na anyeṣām syāt punar śrutiḥ na ca avāntara varṇānām nānātvasya asti kāraṇam na ca ekasya eva sarvāsu gamanam dikṣu yujyate 
[6.113cd_6.116ab]	śrotra āgamana pakṣe ca tat na vṛttiḥ ca gacchati tad adṛṣṭa dvayam tasya dūra sthena ca vikriyā prāptiḥ sarva gata tvāt ced tulyāḥ dūra gateṣu api vikriyā vikriye tatra sarvaiḥ syātām na bhedataḥ asambaddha vikāri tvam api iṣṭam tatra pūrvavat asambandha samāna tve na āsannaḥ hi viśiṣyate 
[6.116cd_6.119ab]	amūrtā śrotra vṛttiḥ ca na mūrtena vihanyate tatra vyavahitaḥ śabdaḥ kim artham na upalabhyate śrtotrasya vikriyāyām ca neyat tāyāḥ niyāmakam na anuvāta ādibhiḥ tasya vṛtteḥ ca preraṇam bhavet anuvātam vihanyeta prativātam ca sā vrajet tad gatam hi anuvāta tvam syāt na śabda gatam tadā 
[6.119cd_6.122cd]	yeṣām tu aprāptaḥ eva ayam śabdaḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyate teṣām aprāpti tulya tvam dūra vyavahita ādiṣu tatra dūra samīpa stha grahaṇa agrahaṇe same syātām na ca kramaḥ na api tīvra manda ādi sambhavaḥ tasmāt śrotriya dṛṣṭā api kalpanā iyam parīkṣyatām prayatna abhihataḥ vāyuḥ koṣṭhyaḥ yāti iti asaṃśayam sa saṃyoga vibhāgau ca tālu ādeḥ anurudhyate 
[6.123ab_6.125cd]	vegavat tvāt ca saḥ avaśyam yāvat vegam pratiṣṭhate tasya ātma vayavānām ca stimitena ca vāyunā saṃyogāḥ viprayogāḥ ca jāyante gamanāt dhruvam karṇa vyomani sa prāptaḥ śaktim śrotre niyacchati tad bhāve śabda bodhāt ca saṃskāraḥ adṛṣṭaḥ iṣyate utpatti śakti vat saḥ api iti adhikam naḥ na kiñ cana 
[6.126ab_6.128cd]	tathā eva tad viśeṣaḥ api viśiṣṭa grahaṇāt bhavet śabda utpatteḥ niṣiddha tvāt anyathā anupapattitaḥ viśiṣṭa saṃskṛteḥ janma dhvanibhyaḥ adhyavasīyate tad bhāva bhāvitā ca atra śakti astitvā avavodhinī śrotra śakti vat eva iṣṭā buddhiḥ tatra hi saṃhṛtā kuḍya ādi pratibandhaḥ api yujyate mātariśvanaḥ 
[6.129ab_6.132ab]	śrotra deśa abhighāte api tena tīvra pravartinā tasya ca krama varti tvāt kṣayi vega ātma saṃpadaḥ saṃskāra krama tīvra tva manda tā ādi nimitta tā imam eva ca saṃskāram śabda grahaṇa kāraṇam ke cit tu paṇḍitam manyāḥ śrotram iti abhimanvate saṃjñā sañcāraṇāt ca eṣām bahu mānaḥ sva cetasi mudhā eṣām bahu mānaḥ ayam vastu anutpādya kiñ cana 
[6.132cd_6.135ab]	dhvani janyāt dhi saṃskārāt śrotram na anyat pradarśitam tam muktvā śrotra śabdena kim dṛṣṭam adhikam ca taiḥ evan jātīyakān arthān phalena pratipāditān lokaḥ saṃskāra śabdena sāmānyena eva jalpati śrotra śabdaḥ viśeṣeṇa tatra avijñāta saṅgatiḥ siddham sva artham parityajya na abhidhānena vartate 
[6.135cd_6.138ab]	ādau aparibhāṣya tvam bhāṣya kāraḥ yat abravīt padārtheṣu bhavet teṣām tad atikramaṇam phalam saṃskāra vyatirikte ca sarva lokasya vastuni śrotra śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ san svāt chandyena apanīyate indriyāṇām abhivyaktiḥ garbha sthasya eva dehinaḥ prāk kāryāt āgamaiḥ siddhā tad pradveṣeṇa laṅghyate 
[6.138cd_6.141ab]	na ca śabda artha sambandhaḥ kartum yogyaḥ kathan cana kṣaṇika śrotra pakṣe ca saḥ avaśyam kṛtakaḥ bhavet saṃskāre tulyam etat ced na saṃskāra antara sthiteḥ saṃskāra śabda vācyā hi ke cit varṣa śatāni api dhriyante tena tad śabda sambandhaḥ na vinaśyati śrotra śabdaḥ punar pūrva saṃskārāt uttaratra tu 
[6.141cd_6.144ab]	eka deśa nibaddhe hi sarvadā arthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ śakyam ca ghriyamāṇa tvam indriya tvāt tvac ādi tvat vaktum śrotrasya tena atra kṣaṇikā utpatti asambhavaḥ yadi ca dhvani sa samparkāt śrotram eva upajāyate badhirasya api tat janma kim artham na upalabhyate yat yasya na asti tat tasya sutarām janana kṣamam 
[6.144cd_6.147ab]	tasmāt apekṣitam śrotram badhirasya api jāyatām saṃskāre api aviśiṣṭam ced na asau upahata indriye śrotram ācchāditam doṣaiḥ saṃskartum dhvanayaḥ akṣamāḥ utpadyamāna pakṣe tu na kiñ cit pratibandhanam śrotram ākāśa deśam ca bhautika indriya vādinaḥ yam āhuḥ tasya sadbhāvaḥ prāc dhvaneḥ kena vāryate 
[6.147cd_6.150cd]	siddhasya ca padārthasya yā ani atas kāryam yogya tā saṃskāra śabda vācya tvāt sā yuktyā vāryate kayā loka āgama prasiddheṣu padārtheṣu anyathā vacaḥ tad mudhā kheda kāri syāt go viṣāṇa aśana upamam yadi tu avaśyam kartavyaḥ tārkika ukti viparyayaḥ tatas veda anusāreṇa kāryā diś śrotra tā matiḥ diśaḥ śrotram iti hi etat pralayeṣu abhidhīyate 
[6.151ab_6.154ab]	tat ca prakṛti gāmi tva vacanam cakṣuḥ ādi vat sūryam asya tathā cakṣuḥ uktam gamayatāt iti tejaḥ prakṛti vijñānam tathā śrotram diś ātmakam diś ca sarvaṃgataukā ca yāvat vyoma vyavasthitā karṇa chidra paricchannā śrtotram ākāśa deśa vat yāvān ca kaṇabhuj nyāyaḥ nabhaḥ bhāga prakalpane digbhāge tu samastaḥ asau āgamāt tu viśiṣyate 
[6.154cd_6.157ab]	tasmāt diś dravya bhāgaḥ yaḥ puṇyā puṇya vaśīkṛtaḥ karṇa chidra paricchinnaḥ śrotram saṃskriyate ca saḥ tasmāt svatas anavasthānam parastāt iti asiddha tā pratyayasya anavasthānam vyomni api sthagite asti naḥ na ca tasmin vināśi tvam dravye adravya ātmake sati tatra anumāna buddhiḥ ced śabde api asti iti gamyatām 
[6.157cd_6.160ab]	karoteḥ yat ca karma tvāt kṛtaka tvam udāhṛtam arthaḥ tāvat asiddhaḥ ayam abhidhānam atha ucyate tatra api vyabhicāri tvam tad kriyā janma vādinaḥ gomaya ādā atat janye api eṣa śabdaḥ hi dṛśyate yathā kathan cit iṣṭam ced kārya tvam gomaya ādiṣu tathā api ākāśa mātra tvam kuruṣu eti atra dṛśyate 
[6.160cd_6.163ab]	varaṇa abhāva mātra tvāt kāryam eva iti ced na tat bauddhānām api na abhāvaḥ svayaṃsiddhaḥ hi janyate mṛdām deśa antara prāptiḥ vyāpāra phalam atra hi anāvṛtya ātmakam vyoma nityam eva vyavasthitam nityasya karaṇa abhāvāt prayoge asmin atha ucyate bhrānta tvam gauṇa tā vā iti śabde api evam bhaviṣyati 
[6.163cd_6.166ab]	prāc bhāgaḥ yaḥ surāṣṭrāṇām mālavānām sa dakṣiṇaḥ prāc bhāgaḥ punar etaṣām teṣām uttaratas sthitaḥ tena sūrya uditeḥ deśau bhinnau ubhaya vāsinām dṛṣṭau savituḥ eka tve api atas anaikāntikaḥ bhavet paśyanti eke ca yat deśau udayāḥ tamayau raveḥ tāvati eva abhimanyante parastāt tad nivāsinaḥ 
[6.166cd_6.169cd]	na ca bhinnāḥ nirīkṣyante tena na āditya bhinna tā madhyāhne sarvam puṃsām syāt ekam ca upari darśanam yaḥ yaḥ gṛhītaḥ sarvasmāt puratas savitā īkṣyate tad antara adhika ātmā ca bhāti tena agratas sthitaḥ viprakṛṣṭa antarāṇām ca stoka deśe api dṛśyate siddha bhinna agra deśānām dūra deśa samāna tā tatra api viprakṛṣṭasya sannidhi adhyāsa kāri tā 
[6.170ab_6.172cd]	deśa bhrāntiḥ bhavet puṃsām tat tad deśam apaśyatām śabde tu kiṃnimittā eṣā tatra api vyāpita akṛtā yaḥ yaḥ gṛhītaḥ sarvasmin deśe śabdaḥ api dṛśyate na ca asya avayavāḥ santi yena vartteta bhāgaśas śabdaḥ varttate iti evam tatra sarva ātmakaḥ ca saḥ vyañjaka dhvanī adhīna tvāt tad deśe tu sa gṛhyate 
[6.173ab_6.176ab]	na ca dhvanīnām sāmarthyam vyāptum vyoma nirantaram tena avicchinna rūpeṇa na asau sarvatra gṛhyate dhvanīnām bhinna deśa tvam śrutiḥ tatra anurudhyate apūrita antarāla tvāt vicchedaḥ ca avasīyate teṣām ca alpaka deśa tvāt śabdasya avibhutā matiḥ gatimat vegavat tvābhyām te ca āyānti yatas yatas śrotā tatas tatas śabdam āyāntam iva manyate 
[6.176cd_6.179cd]	sūryasya bhinna deśa tvam nanu ekena na gṛhyate na nāma sarvathā tāvat dṛṣṭa āsya aneka deśa tā sa viśeṣaṇa hetuḥ ced tathā api vyabhicāritā dṛśyate bhinna deśaḥ ayam iti ekaḥ api hi buddhyate jala pātreṣu ca ekena na anekaḥ savitā īkṣyate yugapad na ca bhedasya pramāṇam tulya vedanāt āha ekena nimittena pratipātram pṛthak pṛthak 
[6.180ab_6.183ab]	bhinnāni pratibimbāni jāyante yugapad mam a atra brūmaḥ yadā tāvat jale saureṇa tejasā sphuratā cākṣuṣam tejaḥ pratisrotas pravarttitam sva deśaḥ eva gṛhṇāti savitāram anekadhā bhinna mūrtim yathā pātram tadā asya aneka tā kutas īṣat nimīlite aṅgulyā yathā cakṣuṣi dṛśyate pṛthak ekaḥ api bhinna tvāt cakṣuḥ vṛtteḥ tathā eva naḥ 
[6.183cd_6.186ab]	anye tu codayanti atra pratibimba udaya eṣiṇaḥ saḥ eva ced pratīyeta kasmāt na upari dṛśyate kūpa ādiṣu kutas adhastāt pratibimba īkṣaṇam bhavet prāṅmukhaḥ darpaṇam paśyan syāt ced pratyaṅmukhaḥ katham tatra eva bodhayet artham bahis yātam yat indriyam tatas etat bhavet evam śarīre tat tu bodhakam 
[6.186cd_6.189ab]	ap sūrya darśinām nityam cakṣuḥ dvedhā pravarttate ekam ūrdhvam adhastāt ca tatra ūrdhva aṃśa prakāśitam adhiṣṭhāna an ṛju stha tvāt na ātmā sūryam prapadyate pāramparya arpitam santam avāgvṛttyā tu budhyate ūrdhva vṛtteḥ tad eka tvāt avāk iva ca manyate adhastāt eva tena arkaḥ sa antarālaḥ pratīyate 
[6.189cd_6.192cd]	evam prāk bhūtayā vṛttyā pratyak vṛtti samarpitam budhyamānaḥ mukham bhrāntyā pratyak iti avagacchati aneka deśa vṛttau vā sati api pratibimbake samāna buddhi gamya tvāt nānātvam na eva vidyate vaktṛ vaktra pradeśānām bhinna tvāt bhinna deśa tā śrotra āgamana pakṣe syāt tad deśe tu eka deśa tā adhiṣṭhānābahis vṛtteḥ anyasmin sati api indriye 
[6.193ab_6.196ab]	tad deśāḥ karṇa śaṣkulyaḥ gṛhyeran gamane sati iyam tu vaktṛ aneka tve śrotra eka tve ca kalpanā vaktari ekatra bhinneṣu śrtotṛṣu syāt viparyayaḥ tatra hi śrotra deśānām bhinna tvāt bhinna deśa tā tad āgame tu vaktrekyāt eka deśa tva sambhavaḥ dhvani āgatyā yadi bhrāntiḥ itaratra api sā samā bhinna vyañjaka tālu ādi deśa bhedāt bhaviṣyati 
[6.196cd_6.199cd]	sūtreṇa yugapad bhāvaḥ śrotra eka tvāt udāhṛtaḥ atas tad anusāreṇa yadi api ityādi kīrtanam deśa bhedena bhinna tvam iti etat ca anumānikam pratyakṣaḥ tu saḥ eva iti pratyayaḥ tena bādhakaḥ paryāyeṇa yathā ca ekaḥ bhinnān deśān vrajan api devadattaḥ na bhidyeta tathā śabdaḥ na bhidyate jñāta ekatvaḥ yathā eva asau dṛśyamānaḥ punar punar 
[6.200ab_6.202cd]	na bhinnaḥ kāla bhedena tathā śabdaḥ na deśataḥ paryāyāt avirodhaḥ ced vyāpi tvāt api dṛśyatām dṛṣṭa siddhau hi yaḥ dharmaḥ sarvathā saḥ abhyupeyate varṇa antara vikārya tvāt iti yoktā vināśitā ukte ca hetu siddhi artha sādṛśya smaraṇe punar tatra smṛteḥ asiddha tvam na hi evam pāṇineḥ vacaḥ 
[6.203ab_6.205cd]	ikāra pariṇāmena yakāraḥ kriyatām iti siddhe śabda artha sambandhe tat śāstram hi pravarttate prayoga niyama arthāya na ca evam siddha tā bhavet bhinna prasiddhayoḥ tena dadhi dadhyā iti śabdayoḥ ācakṣāṇena sādhu tvam dadhīti autsargikaḥ kṛtaḥ anvākhyātum svarūpeṇa dadhyaśabdam ca veditum 
[6.206ab_6.208cd]	sva śāstre laghu bodha artham eka tvam iva darśitam tatra aci paratas siddham dadhyaśabdam nivarttayan dadhi iti śāstrataḥ prāptaḥ saḥ ayam tena eva vāryate ikprayoga prasaṅge tu yaṇ sādhuḥ iti gamyate parama arthaḥ tu na eva asmin vikāraḥ abhūt kadā cana kevalam yat tu sādṛśyam tat anaikāntikīkṛtam 
[6.209ab_6.211cd]	kunde dadhi avikāre api tad sādṛśyam hi dṛśyate na asti sarva ātmanā tat ced śabde api sthāna mātrakam tena etayoḥ asiddhatvāt mūla hetoḥ asiddha tā kāraṇa anuvidhāyi tvam yat ca alpa tva mahat tvayoḥ tat asiddham na varṇaḥ hi vardhate na padam kva cit varṇa antara janau tāvat tad pada tvam vihanyate 
[6.212ab_6.214cd]	apadam hi bhavet etat yadi vā syāt pada antaram varṇaḥ anavayava tvāt tu vṛddhi hrāsau na gacchati vyoma ādi vat atas asiddhāḥ vṛddhiḥ asya svarūpataḥ atha tādrūpya vijñānam hetuḥ iti abhidhīyate tathā api vyabhicāri tvam śabda tve api hi tad matiḥ vyakti alpa tva mahat tve ca yat yathā anuvidhīyate 
[6.215ab_6.217cd]	tathā eva anuvidhāna artham dhvani alpa tva mahat tvayoḥ vyaṅgyānām ca etat asti iti loke api aikāntikam na tat darpaṇa alpa mahat tve api dṛśyate anupatat mukham na syāt avyaṅgyatā tasya tad kriyā janya tā api vā na ca asya uccāraṇāt anyā vidyate janikā kriyā yathā mahatyām khātāyām mṛdi vyomni mahat tva dhīḥ 
[6.218ab_6.221ab]	alpāyām alpa dhīḥ evam atyanta akṛtake sati tena atra evam para upādhiḥ śabda vṛddhau mati bhramaḥ na casyūla tva sūkṣma tve lakṣyete śabda vṛttinī buddhi tīvra tva manda tve mahattva alpa tva kalpanā sā ca paṭvī bhavati eva mahā tejaḥ prakāśite manda prakāśite mandā ghaṭa ādau api sarvadā evam dīrgha ādayaḥ sarve dhvani dharmā iti sthitam 
[6.221cd_6.224ab]	nādaḥ vāyu guṇaḥ tadvān vāyuḥ vā yadi kalpyate varṇānām śrotra gamya tvāt na ca ye śrotra gocarāḥ tatra āvarṇa ātmakaḥ śabdaḥ śaṅkha ādeḥ śrūyate katham dhvanīnām śrotra gamya tvam tasmāt ke cit pracakṣate māruta preritāḥ te ca kurvanti śrotra saṃskṛtim varṇa vyaktau ca dṛṣṭa tvāt teṣām na adṛṣṭa kalpanā 
[6.224cd_6.227ab]	anye tu varṇayanti atra pūrva ukta dhvani vādinaḥ marutām eva nānātvāt ghoṣa śruti upapādanam tatra tālu ādi saṃyoga vibhāgaiḥ preritāḥ sphuṭam vyañjanti varṇam anye tu śabda tvam sarva varṇa bhāj varṇa sarva gata tvāt tu na apadyeta nirāśrayam na ca paryanuyogaḥ syāt kva varṇe vyaktiḥ iti ayam 
[6.227cd_6.230cd]	ete eva ca te pūrvam uktāḥ bodha anuvarttinaḥ yeṣām pracaya nānātvāt vṛtti bhedaḥ pratīyate yat vā jāti antaram santu sarvathā kārya hetukam tvad pakṣa vat dhvanīnām naḥ śakti bheda prakalpanam darśanasya parārtha tvam yadi nāma pratīyate śabdasya kim iha āyātam yena nityaḥ abhyupeyate anityeṣu api dṛṣṭa tvāt dvīpa jvālā ghaṭa ādiṣu 
[6.231ab_6.234ab]	para artha darśana tvasya dharma tve api na hetu tā vinā sādharmya dṛṣṭāntāt viruddhaḥ vā bhavet ayam nityānām aprayogi tvam aṇūnām api daśyate artha pratyāyanam ca eṣa janmanā eva kariṣyati vinā api sthāsnu rūpeṇa saṃyoga ādīn yathā kriyā pūrva ālocanam etasya bhūta smṛtyā ca karma vat tasmāt na viniyojya tvāt prāc astitvam ghaṭa ādi vat 
[6.234cd_6.237cd]	prakāśitam yathā ca artham tejasā kena cit purā na vā bhūyopi buddhi ante śabdāt api tathā bhavet darśanasya parārtha tve yat asiddhi ādi codyate tad kāṣṭha dahanaḥ vahniḥ abdāha artham niyujyate anumāna prayoge hi vaktum ityādi yujyate arthāpattiḥ iyam ca uktā pakṣa dharma ādi varjitā yadi nāśini nitye vā vināśinī eva vā bhavet 
[6.238ab_6.240cd]	śabde vācaka sāmarthyam tatas dūṣaṇam ucyatām phalavat vyavahāra aṅga bhūta artha pratyaya aṅga tā niṣphala tvena śabdasya yogya tvāt avadhāryate parīkṣyamāṇaḥ tena asya yuktyā nitya vināśayoḥ sa dharmaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ yaḥ pradhānam na bādhate na hi aṅga aṅga anurodhena pradhāna phala bādhanam 
[6.241ab_6.243cd]	yujyate na āśi pakṣe ca tad ekāntāt prasajyate na hi adṛṣṭa artha sambandhaḥ śabdaḥ bhavati vācakaḥ tathā ced syāt apūrvaḥ api sarvaḥ sarvam prakāśayet sambandha darśanam ca asya na anityasya upapadyate sambandha jñāna siddhiḥ ced dhruvam kāla antara sthitiḥ anyasmin jñāta sambandhe na ca anyaḥ vācakaḥ bhavet 
[6.244ab_6.247ab]	go śabda ijñāta sambandhe na aśva śabdaḥ hi vācakaḥ atha anyaḥ api svabhāvena kaḥ cit eva avabodhakaḥ tatra anibandhane na syāt kaḥ asau iti viniścayaḥ yatas pratyayaḥ iti evam vyavahāraḥ avakalpate śrotāṇām syāt api ittham tu vaktāṇām na avakalpate ajñātvā kam asau śabdam ādau eva vivakṣati jānāti ced avaśyam sa pūrvam tena avadhāritaḥ 
[6.247cd_6.250ab]	tejaḥ pratyakṣa śeṣa tvāt na tattve api prakāśakam sadṛśa tvāt pratītiḥ ced tad dvāreṇa api avācakaḥ kasya ca ekasya sādṛśyāt kalpyatām vācakaḥ aparaḥ adṛṣṭa saṅgati tvena sarveṣām tulya tā yatas arthavān pūrva dṛṣṭaḥ ced tasya tāvān kutas kṣaṇaḥ dvis tris vā anupalabdhaḥ hi na arthavān sampratīyate 
[6.250cd_6.253ab]	apratīta ani a śabdānām tad kāle asau anarthakaḥ saḥ eva anya śrutīnām syāt arthavān iti vismayaḥ atha asya vidyamānāḥ api kaiḥ cit arthaḥ na gamyate tad tulyam uttarasya iti kim sādṛśyena vācakaḥ anarthaka tvam asya syāt artha ananya śrutīn prati pūrvasmin api tat sattvāt sarva anarthaka tā bhavet 
[6.253cd_6.256cd]	arthavat sadṛśa tvena yaḥ vā śrutavatām mataḥ mukhyaḥ asau aśrutīnām syāt tat eka tve na yujyate sambandha akaraṇe yuktiḥ tat uktam iti kathyate śabda anitya tva pakṣe api viśeṣeṇa sa duṣkaraḥ śabdam tāvat anuccārya sambandha karaṇam kutas na ca uccāritaṣṭasya sambandhena prayojanam tena asambaddhya naṣṭa tvāt pūrvaḥ tāvat anarthakaḥ 
[6.257ab_6.259cd]	uttaraḥ akṛta sambandhaḥ vijñāyeta arthavān katham śabda uccāraṇa sambandha karaṇa vyāvahārikāḥ kriyāḥ krama svabhāva tvāt kaḥ kuryāt yugapad kva cit deśa kāla ādi bhedānām puṃsā śabda antara śruteḥ pūrvam kṛtrima sambandhe api ekaḥ śabdaḥ na sidhyati sambandha kathane api asya syāt eva eṣā nirākṛtiḥ
